The flags are honest: the shim (services/lambda_svc.py) reads cloudwatch Invocations (ARM) and ProvisionedConcurrencyUtilization (PC) and short-circuits both under ctx.fast_mode (lines 128,160,220,247). The doc is accurate but silent on the alias/version metric-dimension gap (finding H1).

**Verdict:** The lambda adapter is cost-correct on every DOLLAR it counts: the only two priced numbers (PC x86/arm64 allocation rates) match the live AWS Pricing API to the digit (SKUs BMKCD2ZCEYKTYYCB / MV7PTBS82AVCMXJJ), are arch-aware, region-scaled exactly once, and gated on a real ProvisionedConcurrencyUtilization datapoint (1-max_util peak). CoH and CO savings are region-priced upstream and not re-multiplied; the CO opt-in placeholder is converted to ctx.warn and dropped; Excessive-Memory and ARM are honestly forced to $0 advisory (Counted=False) with a PricingWarning; cross-source authority dedup is CoH>CO>enhanced on a normalized bare function name; CloudWatch/CO failures are classified to permission_issue vs warn once per scan; fast_mode short-circuits both CW reads. No $ inflation, no double-count, no fabricated free-tier saving, and the per-tab headline (counted total) reconciles with the rendered counted/advisory split. The three remaining material gaps are all in the SAFE (under-report) direction: H1 the PC utilization metric is read with a FunctionName-only dimension while PC always lives on an alias/version, so the one counted enhanced lever frequently degrades to a $0 advisory (highest impact, fixable by adding the Resource dimension); M1 the dedup over-broadly drops the counted PC rec when the same function appears in CoH/CO (a distinct lever those sources never price); and a cluster of LOW limitations (dead Phase B handler, ARM allowlist drift, PC-config pagination, prose-vs-dollar PC card rendering, structurally-$0 Memory/ARM). Nothing rises to CRITICAL; no confirmed false-positive savings.

**Pricing validation:** VALIDATED against the live AWS Pricing API (AWSLambda, us-east-1, publicationDate 2026-06-25). Both module constants are exactly correct and arch-aware: Lambda-Provisioned-Concurrency SKU BMKCD2ZCEYKTYYCB = $0.0000041667/GB-s == _LAMBDA_PC_PRICE_PER_GB_SEC; Lambda-Provisioned-Concurrency-ARM SKU MV7PTBS82AVCMXJJ = $0.0000033334/GB-s == _LAMBDA_PC_PRICE_PER_GB_SEC_ARM (ratio 0.8, i.e. exactly 20% cheaper, and arch selects the rate at lambda_svc.py:164-167). These are the PC ALLOCATION dimensions (group AWS-Lambda-Provisioned-Concurrency), correctly distinct from the execution-on-PC duration dimensions Lambda-Provisioned-GB-Second ($0.0000097222 x86) / -ARM ($0.0000077778) and from standard on-demand duration ($0.0000166667 x86), all of which the code comment (lambda_svc.py:17-26) cites accurately. The formula uses the allocation rate x 730h x 3600s x mem_gb x pc_count for the 24/7 allocation, region-scaled exactly once via ctx.pricing_multiplier at the emit site (line 178) and confirmed single-applied by test_pc_region_multiplier_applied_once. CoH and CO savings are region-priced upstream and NOT re-multiplied (advisor.py:383). No rate inaccuracy found; the only PC issue is the metric-dimension gap (H1) that suppresses the saving, not mis-prices it.

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
