- **Evidence:** _render_opensearch_enhanced_checks groups recs by CheckCategory and prints domains[0].get('EstimatedSavings') (L1111-1113) - the shim string '100% of domain cost' / '30-50%' / 'Estimated: 20-40%' - never the per-rec EstimatedMonthlySavings float the adapter computed (opensearch.py L65). It also never reads 'Counted', so advisory $0 recs (Reserved, Idle, Underutilized) render identically to counted ones, and only ONE string per category is shown even when per-domain dollars differ. The tab/headline total comes from total_monthly_savings (html_report_generator.py _calculate_service_savings L3076-3079).
- **Impact:** Guaranteed counted != rendered desync: cards advertise a percentage (e.g. '100% of domain cost' for an idle domain that contributed $0), while the headline sums dollars. Advisory recs are visually indistinguishable from counted ones.
- **Fix:** Render per-domain rec['EstimatedMonthlySavings'] for Counted recs and tag Counted=False recs as 'advisory'; reconcile the card sum to total_monthly_savings.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified. _render_opensearch_enhanced_checks (reporter_phase_b.py L1092-1129) groups recs by CheckCategory and prints savings_str = domains[0].get('EstimatedSavings','') (L1111-1113) — the shim human string ('100% of domain cost' / '30-50%' / 'Estimated: 20-40%'), never the per-rec EstimatedMonthlySavings float set by the adapter at L65. The function never reads 'Counted', so advisory $0 recs render identically to counted ones, and only one string per category is shown even when per-domain dollars differ. Counted vs rendered desync confirmed; the tab/headline dollars come from total_monthly_savings via html_report_generator._calculate_service_savings.

#### 🟠 H3 · gp3 storage constant understated and savings-factor mismatched to the gp2->gp3 trigger  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✏️ revised**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/opensearch.py:13-15, 58-60`
- **Evidence:** GP3_PRICE_PER_GB_MONTH=0.11 (L13) vs LIVE AmazonES ES:GP3-Storage = $0.122/GB-mo (validated, us-east-1, operation=ESDomain) -> understated ~10%. The check fires on storage_type=='gp2' (gp2->gp3 migration), whose true delta is ES:GP2-Storage $0.135 - ES:GP3-Storage $0.122 = $0.013/GB-mo (~9.6% of gp2). The adapter instead bills EBS x 0.11 x 0.20 = $0.022/GB-mo (~1.7x the real delta). STORAGE_SAVINGS_FACTOR's docstring (L14, 'cold-tier / UltraWarm') is wrong for a gp2->gp3 rec; UltraWarm/Managed storage is ES:Managed-Storage $0.024/GB-mo (validated, ~80% cut vs gp3), unrelated to the trigger.
- **Impact:** Storage savings overstated ~1.7x per GB; the description (services/opensearch.py L36-39 '20% cost savings') and the factor rationale do not match the real ~9.6% gp2->gp3 delta.
- **Fix:** Replace with the real delta: EBS x (gp2_rate - gp3_rate) via PricingEngine (or constants 0.135/0.122 x pricing_multiplier). Remove the misleading UltraWarm docstring; if an UltraWarm tiering saving is wanted, model it separately at $0.024/GB-mo.
- **Verifier (revised):** The code-level defect is real and confirmed: the adapter computes gp2->gp3 storage savings as ebs * GP3_PRICE_PER_GB_MONTH(0.11) * multiplier * STORAGE_SAVINGS_FACTOR(0.20) (L13/15/58-60) = 0.022/GB-mo, i.e. a flat 20% of the gp3 BASE price, not the gp2-gp3 price DELTA that a migration actually saves; and the STORAGE_SAVINGS_FACTOR docstring (L14, 'cold-tier / UltraWarm storage savings vs gp3') misattributes the factor to a different optimization than the gp2->gp3 trigger it is applied to (services/opensearch.py L111-121). However, the finding's load-bearing QUANTITATIVE claims — constant understated ~10% vs live $0.122, true delta $0.135-$0.122=$0.013, savings overstated ~1.7x — cannot be confirmed from code and require live AWS Pricing validation. The direction of the error is not even determinable from code: applying 0.20*gp3 to standard EBS prices ($0.08 gp3 vs $0.10 gp2) would UNDERstate the delta, so the sign depends on the actual OpenSearch-managed gp2/gp3 prices. Mechanism/impact magnitude as stated is not code-substantiated.  _Correction:_ Real modeling defect (HIGH->retain as code smell, magnitude unverified): gp2->gp3 savings are computed as a flat 20% of the gp3 base price (0.11/GB-mo) rather than as the (gp2_price - gp3_price) migration delta, and the STORAGE_SAVINGS_FACTOR docstring rationale ('cold-tier / UltraWarm') does not match the gp2->gp3 trigger it is used for. Whether this over- or under-states the true saving, and by how much (the asserted ~1.7x and the ~10% understated constant), depends on live OpenSearch-managed EBS gp2/gp3 prices and was not verifiable from the code.

#### 🟠 H4 · Headline fabricates $50/recommendation when the adapter nets $0 (opensearch in _FLAT_SAVINGS_SERVICES)  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `html_report_generator.py:82, 3076-3079, 3092-3094, 3113-3119`
- **Evidence:** _FLAT_SAVINGS_SERVICES includes 'opensearch' (L82). _calculate_service_savings returns the canonical total_monthly_savings only when >0 (L3078-3079); when the adapter nets $0 it falls through and adds +50 per recommendation (L3093-3094) and overwrites service_data['total_monthly_savings'] (L3117-3119). Because C2/C3 zero out idle+underutilized, a region whose domains are all-idle or already-Graviton nets $0 from the adapter yet still has advisory recs (Reserved/Idle), so the headline back-fills $50 x rec_count.
- **Impact:** Fabricated, non-account-specific dollars in the executive summary that directly contradict the adapter's careful $0 gating - exactly the cases C2/C3 zero are the cases this back-fills with a flat $50.
- **Fix:** Remove 'opensearch' from _FLAT_SAVINGS_SERVICES so the headline trusts the adapter float; surface advisory-only regions as $0, not $50/rec.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified. _FLAT_SAVINGS_SERVICES includes 'opensearch' (html_report_generator.py L82). _calculate_service_savings returns the canonical total_monthly_savings only when >0 (L3078-3079); otherwise it falls through and, for each recommendation, adds +50 when service_key in _FLAT_SAVINGS_SERVICES (L3092-3094). _get_service_content then overwrites service_data['total_monthly_savings'] with this calculated value when >0 (L3113-3119), and the reconciliation footnote (L2281-2286) plus other render paths (L2831, L3578) also use _calculate_service_savings. Because C2/C3 zero out idle and underutilized recs, a region whose domains are all-idle / already-Graviton nets $0 from the adapter yet still emits advisory recs (Reserved/Idle/Underutilized), so the report back-fills $50 x rec_count — fabricated, non-account-specific dollars that directly contradict the adapter's $0 gating. Confirmed.

#### 🟡 M1 · CloudWatch read not fast_mode-gated; requires_cloudwatch / reads_fast_mode undeclared  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/opensearch.py + services/opensearch.py:opensearch.py 18-27 (no overrides); services/opensearch.py 123-139`
- **Evidence:** The shim calls cloudwatch.get_metric_statistics (AWS/ES CPUUtilization) unconditionally for every domain (services/opensearch.py L127-139) with no ctx.fast_mode check. OpensearchModule does not override requires_cloudwatch / reads_fast_mode (defaults False in services/_base.py L24-25), and required_clients() omits 'cloudwatch'.
- **Impact:** Per-domain CloudWatch calls run even under fast_mode (latency/cost), diverging from the Lambda/RDS fast-mode pattern; the cloudwatch dependency is undeclared.
- **Fix:** Declare requires_cloudwatch=True, reads_fast_mode=True; skip the metric read (idle/underutilized checks) when ctx.fast_mode is set; add 'cloudwatch' to required_clients().

#### 🟡 M2 · Silent failures: per-domain describe/CloudWatch errors are logger-only; permission errors not classified  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/opensearch.py:166-168, 170-171, 173-174`
- **Evidence:** Inner describe_domain except (L170-171) uses logger.warning only -> a permission/throttle failure makes the whole domain VANISH from the report with no ctx.warn. The CloudWatch except (L166-168) logger.warning + continue silently drops the idle/underutilized checks for that domain. The outer except (L173-174) calls ctx.warn but does NOT classify AccessDenied/UnauthorizedOperation/OptInRequired to ctx.permission_issue (canonical class).
- **Impact:** AccessDenied/throttle on describe_domain or GetMetricStatistics silently removes domains/checks from the report with no surfaced warning -> invisible coverage gaps.
- **Fix:** Route the inner excepts through ctx.warn / ctx.permission_issue (mirror services/_aws_errors.record_aws_error: AccessDenied/Unauthorized/OptInRequired -> permission_issue, else warn); never let a domain disappear logger-only.

#### 🟡 M3 · Flat reduction factors (Graviton 0.25, downsize 0.30) with no target instance/size  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/opensearch.py:46-49, 61-64`
- **Evidence:** rate_by_category applies monthly x factor (0.25 Graviton, 0.30 downsize) with no recorded target instance type/size and no current->target price delta (contrast the EC2 audit mandate of exact current-target; EC2 precedent had factors off 2-3x). No AuditBasis is attached to the counted figure.
- **Impact:** Undefended savings numbers not reproducible from the report; risk of 2-3x error vs a concrete Graviton or one-size-down delta.
- **Fix:** Compute Graviton saving as price(x86 type) - price(Graviton equivalent) and downsize as price(current) - price(one-size-down) via get_instance_monthly_price, recording a structured AuditBasis (rate/region/formula); else keep as $0 advisory.

#### 🟡 M4 · Instance pricing-miss silently zeroes a real saving (no fallback on instance path)  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/opensearch.py + core/pricing_engine.py:opensearch.py 61-64, 87; pricing_engine.py 740-752`
- **Evidence:** get_instance_monthly_price returns _use_fallback(0.0,...) on a Pricing API miss (pricing_engine.py L746-750) - no region-scaled constant fallback. A graviton rec priced 0.0 is then dropped by the keep>0 guard (opensearch.py L87) with no warning.
- **Impact:** A transient Pricing API miss silently drops an otherwise-counted instance saving; no ctx.warn distinguishes 'no saving' from 'could not price'.
- **Fix:** Distinguish a pricing miss (warn/advisory) from a true $0; consider a region-scaled fallback monthly constant for the AmazonES instance path.

#### 🟡 M5 · Serverless / UltraWarm / dedicated-master not priced; 0-node / empty ClusterConfig unguarded  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/opensearch.py:76-79, 93-105`
- **Evidence:** The shim reads only ClusterConfig.InstanceType / InstanceCount (data tier, L76-77) and EBSOptions (L78-79). OpenSearch Serverless collections are not enumerated by list_domain_names and a domain with empty ClusterConfig yields InstanceType='' (not Graviton -> a graviton rec is still appended L96-105) and InstanceCount=0; UltraWarm/cold (ES:Managed-Storage $0.024/GB-mo) and dedicated-master nodes are never costed.
- **Impact:** Serverless (OCU-priced) and UltraWarm savings are missed; a 0-node/empty-ClusterConfig domain emits a graviton rec that prices to $0 and renders an empty advisory card (mirror the EKS 0-node guard).
- **Fix:** Guard InstanceCount<=0 / empty InstanceType before emitting instance recs; document Serverless/UltraWarm/master as out-of-scope or price them via OCU / ES:Managed-Storage.

#### 🟢 L1 · Generic instance price filter does not pin operation; MaxResults=1 (low risk in practice)  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `core/pricing_engine.py:1290-1298, 1601`
- **Evidence:** _fetch_generic_instance_price filters only instanceType + location (L1291-1294) and _call_pricing_api uses MaxResults=1 (L1601) with no operation=ESDomain pin. Live validation: querying AmazonES instanceType='r6g.large.search' returns exactly ONE product SKU (operation=ESDomain, usagetype=ESInstance:r6g.large, $0.167/hr), so MaxResults=1 is deterministic here. A legacy Elasticsearch domain whose ClusterConfig.InstanceType ends in '.elasticsearch' would not match the '.search' SKU -> price 0.0.
- **Impact:** Non-determinism risk is low for OpenSearch (one SKU per instanceType), but legacy '.elasticsearch'-suffixed types silently price to $0.
- **Fix:** Optionally pin operation='ESDomain'; normalize legacy '.elasticsearch' suffix to '.search' before the lookup.

#### 🟢 L2 · CLAUDE.md mislabels opensearch as pure 'Keyword-based' and omits the CoH wiring  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/CLAUDE.md:Parse-rate table row 'opensearch.py | Keyword-based'`
- **Evidence:** The doc files opensearch.py under 'Parse-rate (5 adapters) / Keyword-based', but the adapter does live AmazonES instance pricing (opensearch.py L61-64) + a storage module constant (L13,60) and emits NO text-parsed dollars. The row also omits that opensearch is in scan_orchestrator _HUB_SERVICES/type_map.
- **Impact:** Documentation does not match reality; obscures the orphaned-CoH (C1) and hybrid-pricing behavior.
- **Fix:** Update the row to 'hybrid keyword + live AmazonES instance pricing + gp3 storage constant', and note CoH consumption once C1 is fixed.

### QuickSight — `services/adapters/quicksight.py`

**Module identity:** Identity matches services/adapters/CLAUDE.md and the brief: key="quicksight", cli_aliases=("quicksight",), display_name="QuickSight", required_clients()=("quicksight",) (quicksight.py lines 15-21). Inherits BaseServiceModule defaults (services/_base.py lines 22-26): stat_cards=(), grouping=None, requires_cloudwatch=False, reads_fast_mode=False — all correct (no CloudWatch read; SPICE util comes from describe_spice_capacity). Emits ONE SourceBlock "enhanced_checks" (quicksight.py line 60). Not in PHASE_B_HANDLERS, not in _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC, not in PHASE_A_DESCRIPTORS, not in html descriptor table → renders via render_generic_per_rec → _render_generic_other_rec (confirmed visible, NOT a blank-card service). Consumes neither Cost Optimization Hub nor Compute Optimizer (not in scan_orchestrator _HUB_SERVICES/type_map) — correct per brief, so no missing-CoH/CO finding. DOC RECONCILE MISMATCH: the CLAUDE.md row says "SPICE tier pricing ($0.25-$0.38/GB) | Module constants", implying an edition-aware tier, but the code hardcodes a SINGLE flat $0.38 (quicksight.py line 42) and never applies the documented $0.25 Standard rate. The doc's range is closer to reality than the code; the code regressed to a flat Enterprise rate.

**Verdict:** QuickSight is a thin two-layer adapter: services/adapters/quicksight.py does the dollar math, services/quicksight.py (get_enhanced_quicksight_checks) does detection. Exactly ONE check is live (spice_optimization); user_optimization and capacity_optimization buckets are declared but dead. The single counted formula is UnusedSpiceCapacityGB * SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB(flat 0.38) * pricing_multiplier. CRITICAL bug C1: the flat $0.38 is edition-blind and the code comment wrongly claims it applies to both editions; the live Pricing API confirms Standard SPICE = $0.25/GB-Mo (USE1-QS-Provisioned-SPICE) vs Enterprise $0.38 (USE1-QS-Enterprise-SPICE), so every Standard-edition account's counted saving is 52% too high — and the real edition (describe_account_subscription().AccountInfo.Edition) is never read; the rec's 'Edition' is actually the SPICE PurchaseMode (L1). Two HIGH silent-failure bugs: describe_spice_capacity is wrapped in except:pass (H1) and per-namespace list_users in except:continue (H2) — both can drop the entire dollar-bearing finding with no ctx.warn/permission_issue even though ScanContext exposes both. HIGH H3: the helper's '~$X/month' display string is computed with a bare *0.38 and no region multiplier while the counted numeric is region-scaled, so card text and headline diverge outside us-east-1 (and the generic renderer prints both numbers on the same card). MEDIUM: free included SPICE allotment / removable floor ignored (M1) and the entire per-user author/reader cost lever is unimplemented (M2, dead buckets). Rendering wiring is otherwise correct — quicksight falls through should_fallback_to_per_rec to render_generic_per_rec/_render_generic_other_rec and IS visible (no blank-card bug), and the counted total sums the region-scaled numeric. Read-only audit; no files modified. Phase 7 live scan not run (no AWS credentials in this read-only session) — findings are from static trace + live Pricing API.

**Pricing validation:** Validated against LIVE AWS Pricing API (mcp aws-pricing get_pricing, service_code=AmazonQuickSight, region=us-east-1, publicationDate 2026-06-12). SPICE is edition-priced: USE1-QS-Enterprise-SPICE (attributes.edition=Enterprise) = $0.3800/GB-Mo, SKU R8PKSKFCHES8YSKK; USE1-QS-Provisioned-SPICE (attributes.edition=Standard) = $0.2500/GB-Mo, SKU T4GAEKP5WQQWCUD5. This DIRECTLY CONTRADICTS the adapter's flat SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB=0.38 and its comment that $0.38 applies to BOTH editions: Standard accounts are over-charged 52% (0.38 vs 0.25). Per-user lever (M2) also validated: USE1-Reader-Enterprise-Month = $3.0000/User (SKU B23WCNJ3RN5TAJRH); USE1-Reader-Pro-Enterprise-Month = $20.0000/User (SKU YVR4TMSPWDQHPZH8). Region scaling on the counted path (constant * ctx.pricing_multiplier, quicksight.py line 45) is the correct single-multiply pattern (no PricingEngine call here); the display string omits the multiplier (H3).

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
|---|---|---|---|
| spice_optimization | counted | describe_spice_capacity: total_capacity>0 AND used_capacity < total_capacity*0.5 (>=50% idle), gated by AccountSubscriptionStatus==ACCOUNT_CREATED and total_users>0 (services/quicksight.py lines 37,55,63) | Numeric counted path (adapter): UnusedSpiceCapacityGB(=total-used GB) * SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB(0.38 flat) * ctx.pricing_multiplier (quicksight.py lines 45-50). Display string (helper): bare (total-used)*0.38 with NO multiplier (services/quicksight.py lines 77-81). Both flat $0.38 regardless of edition. |
| user_optimization | advisory | Bucket declared in checks dict (services/quicksight.py line 29) but NEVER populated — dead code | None — no author/reader cost lever implemented; emits nothing |
| capacity_optimization | advisory | Bucket declared in checks dict (services/quicksight.py line 30) but NEVER populated — dead code | None — emits nothing |

**Findings:**

#### 🔴 C1 · Edition-blind flat SPICE rate overcharges every Standard-edition account by 52%  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/quicksight.py:38-50`
- **Evidence:** Line 42: `SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB: float = 0.38` applied to ALL accounts; line 45 `spice_price = SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB * ctx.pricing_multiplier`; lines 48-50 count `unused_gb * spice_price` into total_monthly_savings. Code comment lines 38-40 asserts '$0.38/GB-month for BOTH Standard and Enterprise editions ... Previous code used $0.25 for Standard - wrong by 34%' — a regression in the wrong direction. LIVE AWS Pricing API (AmazonQuickSight us-east-1, 2026-06-12): USE1-QS-Enterprise-SPICE edition=Enterprise = $0.3800/GB-Mo (SKU R8PKSKFCHES8YSKK); USE1-QS-Provisioned-SPICE edition=Standard = $0.2500/GB-Mo (SKU T4GAEKP5WQQWCUD5). The account edition is available from describe_account_subscription().AccountInfo.Edition but the helper reads only AccountSubscriptionStatus (services/quicksight.py line 37), never Edition.
- **Impact:** For every Standard-edition account the counted EstimatedMonthlySavings (which sums into the report headline and executive total via core/result_builder.py line 72) is overstated by (0.38-0.25)/0.25 = 52%. The dollar figure is fabricated-high for an entire account class.
- **Fix:** Resolve edition via describe_account_subscription().AccountInfo.Edition (STANDARD/ENTERPRISE/ENTERPRISE_AND_Q); pin the SPICE rate per-edition ($0.25 Standard SKU T4GAEKP5WQQWCUD5 vs $0.38 Enterprise SKU R8PKSKFCHES8YSKK) via a pinned-filter Pricing lookup. If edition cannot be resolved, mark the rec Counted=False (advisory) rather than silently counting at the Enterprise rate.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** All claims verified in real code plus live pricing. services/adapters/quicksight.py line 42 hardcodes SPICE_PRICE_PER_GB=0.38; line 45 spice_price = 0.38 * ctx.pricing_multiplier; lines 47-50 multiply unused_gb by it into `savings` for EVERY rec with no edition branch. The rec carries no account-edition discriminator the adapter consults. The helper at services/quicksight.py line 37 reads only AccountInfo.AccountSubscriptionStatus and never AccountInfo.Edition (which DescribeAccountSubscription does return), so edition is available but discarded. The `savings` total flows to ServiceFindings.total_monthly_savings (adapter line 65) and is summed into the headline at core/result_builder.py line 72. The load-bearing price claim is confirmed by the LIVE AWS Pricing API (AmazonQuickSight, us-east-1): SKU R8PKSKFCHES8YSKK edition=Enterprise = $0.3800/GB-Mo and SKU T4GAEKP5WQQWCUD5 edition=Standard = $0.2500/GB-Mo — exactly the SKUs/prices cited. The in-code comment (lines 38-40) asserting $0.38 for BOTH editions is factually wrong. Standard-edition accounts are overstated by (0.38-0.25)/0.25 = 52%. The finding correctly scopes the overcharge to Standard accounts (Enterprise's 0.38 is correct), so CRITICAL severity holds.

#### 🟠 H1 · describe_spice_capacity failure swallowed silently (except: pass) — whole SPICE finding vanishes  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:57-86`
- **Evidence:** The entire SPICE block (describe_spice_capacity + the append) is wrapped in `try: ... except Exception: pass` (lines 56,85-86). No ctx.warn / ctx.permission_issue. ScanContext exposes both ctx.warn and ctx.permission_issue (core/scan_context.py lines 49,59) but neither is called here.
- **Impact:** A quicksight:DescribeSpiceCapacity AccessDenied/Unauthorized, throttle, or transient error makes the only revenue-producing check disappear with zero operator signal — the account shows $0 QuickSight savings indistinguishable from a healthy account.
- **Fix:** Replace except:pass with classified handling: AccessDenied/UnauthorizedOperation/OptInRequired -> ctx.permission_issue('quicksight','quicksight:DescribeSpiceCapacity'); other -> ctx.warn(..., 'quicksight').
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified at services/quicksight.py. The SPICE block (try at line 56, describe_spice_capacity at line 57, the only rec append at lines 64-84) is closed by `except Exception: pass` at lines 85-86 with no ctx.warn / ctx.permission_issue inside. This inner handler swallows the exception BEFORE it can reach the outer handler (lines 88-93) that would have called ctx.warn — so a DescribeSpiceCapacity AccessDenied/throttle/transient error drops the only revenue-producing check silently. ScanContext.warn and ScanContext.permission_issue both exist (core/scan_context.py lines 49 and 59) and neither is invoked in the block. Mechanism and HIGH severity accurate; the cited 'lines 57-86' is correct (try opens at 56, except at 85-86).

#### 🟠 H2 · Per-namespace list_users failure (except: continue) silently under-counts users and can suppress the entire SPICE check  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:46-55`
- **Evidence:** Lines 48-53: `try: paginator...list_users... except Exception: continue`. total_users accumulates across namespaces; line 55 gates the whole SPICE block on `if total_users > 0`. A namespace whose list_users throws (e.g. quicksight:ListUsers AccessDenied/throttle) is skipped with no ctx record; if all namespaces fail, total_users stays 0 and the SPICE recommendation is suppressed entirely.
- **Impact:** Silent under-count flips total_users>0 to false and drops a real, dollar-bearing SPICE recommendation with no warning — a permission gap masquerades as 'no opportunity'.
- **Fix:** Record the per-namespace failure on ctx (permission_issue for AccessDenied, else warn) instead of bare continue; consider that an inability to enumerate users should not silently zero out an account-level SPICE check.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified at services/quicksight.py lines 45-55. total_users initialized at line 45; per-namespace list_users pagination at lines 49-51 is wrapped in `try ... except Exception: continue` (lines 48-53) with no ctx.warn/permission_issue. Line 55 gates the entire SPICE block on `if total_users > 0`. If every namespace's ListUsers throws (AccessDenied/throttle), total_users stays 0 and the SPICE recommendation is suppressed with zero operator signal — a permission gap presents as 'no opportunity'. Confirmed as described; HIGH severity reasonable.

#### 🟠 H3 · Display string (non-region-scaled, flat $0.38) disagrees with counted numeric on the same card  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:77-81`
- **Evidence:** Helper writes EstimatedSavings = f'~${(total_capacity - used_capacity) * 0.38:.0f}/month' with NO ctx.pricing_multiplier (lines 77-81), while the adapter writes numeric EstimatedMonthlySavings = unused * 0.38 * ctx.pricing_multiplier (quicksight.py line 45-49). The renderer _render_generic_other_rec dumps EVERY rec key as <p> lines (reporter_phase_b.py lines 1865-1869) — so the region-scaled numeric EstimatedMonthlySavings AND the non-scaled string EstimatedSavings (line 1874-1875) both appear on the same card. The headline counts the numeric (core/result_builder.py line 72).
- **Impact:** In any non-us-east-1 region the card shows two different savings numbers and the rendered '~$X/month' string disagrees with the counted headline number. (Standard accounts: both are also wrong-rate per C1.)
- **Fix:** Make a single region-scaled, edition-correct source of truth and have the helper string and the adapter numeric derive from it; record a structured AuditBasis (rate/region/edition/used-vs-total GB/formula) on the counted finding.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified end-to-end. services/quicksight.py lines 77-81 set EstimatedSavings = f'~${(total_capacity - used_capacity) * 0.38:.0f}/month' with NO ctx.pricing_multiplier; services/adapters/quicksight.py lines 45-49 set numeric EstimatedMonthlySavings = unused * 0.38 * ctx.pricing_multiplier on the same rec. Routing confirmed: quicksight has NO (quicksight, enhanced_checks) entry in PHASE_B_HANDLERS (reporter_phase_b.py lines 2436-2498) and is NOT in _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC (lines 2516-2530), so should_use_handler() is False and should_fallback_to_per_rec() is True (html_report_generator.py lines 3337-3362) → render_generic_per_rec → else branch → _render_generic_other_rec (reporter_phase_b.py line 1381). In _render_generic_other_rec the key-dump loop (lines 1865-1869) prints EstimatedMonthlySavings as a generic <p> (it is a truthy float, not in the skip list, doesn't end in 'Arn'), and EstimatedSavings is printed separately at lines 1874-1875. Both keys are present on the rec, so in any non-us-east-1 region (pricing_multiplier != 1.0) the card shows two diverging savings numbers, and the headline counts the region-scaled numeric (result_builder.py line 72). Confirmed; HIGH severity accurate.

#### 🟡 M1 · Free included SPICE allotment ignored — saving treats all headroom as recoverable cash  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/quicksight.py:46-50`
- **Evidence:** Saving = rate * (total - used) (UnusedSpiceCapacityGB = total - used, services/quicksight.py line 70). Enterprise edition includes a per-paid-author free SPICE allotment (historically 10 GB/author) and a per-reader allotment that is not separately netted out. The formula counts the entire idle headroom as billable.
- **Impact:** Over-states the realizable saving by up to (included_free_GB * rate); an account whose idle GB is mostly within the included free allotment shows a saving it cannot actually realize.
- **Fix:** Floor the saving to max(0, total - used - included_free_GB) * rate, deriving included_free_GB from paid author/reader counts; record the allotment in the AuditBasis. (Needs author/reader counts which the helper already could obtain from list_users.)

#### 🟡 M2 · Whole per-user cost lever (idle authors / never-logged-in readers) is unimplemented — dead buckets  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:27-31`
- **Evidence:** checks dict declares user_optimization and capacity_optimization (lines 29-30) but they are never appended to; only spice_optimization is populated. No author/reader pricing exists. LIVE Pricing API confirms real money: USE1-Reader-Enterprise-Month = $3.00/User (SKU B23WCNJ3RN5TAJRH), Reader Pro = $20/User (SKU YVR4TMSPWDQHPZH8); Enterprise authors ~$18-24/mo.
- **Impact:** A QuickSight account with idle/over-provisioned authors or never-logged-in readers but well-utilized SPICE produces ZERO recommendations — a large cost category is invisible.
- **Fix:** Populate user_optimization from list_users + per-user last-login activity evidence, pricing authors/readers at edition-correct SKUs; keep it evidence-gated (not config-only). Mark as advisory until activity evidence exists.

#### 🟢 L1 · Rec 'Edition' field is the SPICE PurchaseMode, not the billing edition, and defaults to ENTERPRISE  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:71`
- **Evidence:** Line 71: 'Edition': capacity_config.get('PurchaseMode', 'ENTERPRISE'). PurchaseMode is the SPICE purchase mode, not AccountInfo.Edition. The renderer prints it as 'Edition: <value>' (_render_generic_other_rec, reporter_phase_b.py lines 1865-1869).
- **Impact:** The card presents a mislabeled value as the billing edition, defaulting to ENTERPRISE — reinforces the C1 over-charge narrative and misleads anyone validating the rate from the report.
- **Fix:** Set Edition from describe_account_subscription().AccountInfo.Edition; rename the PurchaseMode field if it must be shown.

#### 🟢 L2 · $0-advisory branch sets PricingWarning but no Counted=False (would be tallied as 'counted' if reached)  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/quicksight.py:51-58`
- **Evidence:** else branch sets EstimatedMonthlySavings=0.0 + PricingWarning but does NOT set Counted=False. _counted_advisory_counts (html_report_generator.py lines 371-388) classifies a rec as advisory ONLY when Counted is False; otherwise it is counted. In current wiring the helper always sets UnusedSpiceCapacityGB on every emitted rec (services/quicksight.py line 70), so this branch is effectively unreachable today, but it is latent.
- **Impact:** If ever reached, a $0 rec would inflate the 'N counted' tally in the tab header while contributing $0 to the dollar total — counted-count vs counted-dollars desync.
- **Fix:** Set rec['Counted'] = False on the $0/PricingWarning path so it renders as advisory.

#### 🟢 L3 · Hard 50%-idle trigger excludes accounts with material but <50% idle SPICE  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/quicksight.py:63`
- **Evidence:** Line 63: `if total_capacity > 0 and used_capacity < total_capacity * 0.5`. An account at 40% idle (60% utilized) is excluded even though 40% idle of a large SPICE pool is real recoverable money. The saving itself is correctly grounded in measured UnusedSpiceCapacityGB (line 70), so this is purely a trigger-threshold coverage gap, not a fabricated number.
- **Impact:** Under-coverage: real idle SPICE between 0-50% idle yields no recommendation.
- **Fix:** Treat the 50% as a flag heuristic and emit a (possibly advisory) recommendation for any meaningfully idle headroom, with the saving still derived from measured unused GB.

### RDS — `services/adapters/rds.py`

**Module identity:** MATCHES services/adapters/CLAUDE.md. services/adapters/rds.py:42-50 — key="rds", cli_aliases=("rds",), display_name="RDS", requires_cloudwatch=True, reads_fast_mode=True, required_clients()=("rds","compute-optimizer","cloudwatch","ce"). Consistent with brief 0b. CLAUDE.md rds.py row claims all confirmed: Multi-AZ-disable & non-prod scheduling CloudWatch-gated on DatabaseConnections (services/rds.py:33-57, 365-392, 437-444, 557-561); no gp2->gp3 check (services/rds.py:538-545; gp2==gp3 re-validated live); backup retention advisory (rds_logic.py:24-25, services/rds.py:504-536); Aurora-aware snapshot rate $0.021 vs $0.095 (services/rds.py:106-115, pricing_engine.py:639-666) and Aurora storage-mode SKU on instance pricing (pricing_engine.py:1184-1188); intentional coverage gaps Serverless v2/cluster-rightsizing/read-replicas/stopped/Extended-Support (services/rds.py:326-333, 604-607, 665-666, 722-725). Minor doc lag only: CLAUDE.md signature omits the aurora_io_optimized kwarg now present on get_rds_instance_monthly_price. No material drift.

**Verdict:** RDS is the mature multi-source aggregator the brief describes and most invariants hold: cross-source authority CoH>CO>heuristic with normalized-ARN keys, single highest-savings finding per DB (Multi-AZ vs scheduling cannot stack), snapshots on independent keys, RI + backup-retention correctly demoted to advisory (ADVISORY_CATEGORIES + _coh_is_renderable filtering PurchaseReservedInstances/PurchaseSavingsPlans/N-A), CO opt-in placeholder converted to ctx.warn and dropped, all three sources (compute_optimizer, enhanced_checks, cost_optimization_hub) have PHASE_B handlers, counted==rendered (per-service total flows from resolve_rds_findings into _calculate_service_savings without re-derivation), full pagination on all four describe_* calls, no double-region bug, and permission/CE/CloudWatch failures classified to ctx.permission_issue/ctx.warn. Live Pricing API confirmed the three material rates ($0.095 standard backup, $0.021 Aurora backup, gp2==gp3 $0.115) so the hardcoded fallbacks and the gp2->gp3 omission are correct. The one HIGH issue is the documented Aurora cross-tab overlap: provisioned Aurora member instances can be counted in both the RDS tab (CO/CoH) and the Aurora tab (aurora.py rightsizing/Graviton) with no cross-adapter covered set, and result_builder sums both into the headline (H1, confirmed_bug). Remaining items are minor: scheduling's fixed 0.65 reduction factor feeds the counted total (M1, tradeoff), the backup advisory hardcodes the standard rate for Aurora (L1, cosmetic), scheduling's name-only gate ignores the Environment tag (L2), and Multi-AZ lacks the Aurora exclusion scheduling has (L3). The documented coverage gaps (Serverless v2/ACU, cluster rightsizing, read replicas, stopped instances, Extended Support) are genuine tradeoffs owned elsewhere, not leakage.

**Pricing validation:** Validated live against AWS Pricing API (AmazonRDS, us-east-1, publicationDate 2026-06-19) via get_pricing. (1) Standard RDS backup: productFamily=Storage Snapshot, databaseEngine=MySQL, usagetype RDS:ChargedBackupUsage = $0.0950/GB-Mo -> matches FALLBACK_RDS_BACKUP_GB_MONTH=0.095 and services/rds.py _backup_rate. (2) Aurora backup: databaseEngine=Aurora MySQL, usagetype Aurora:BackupUsage = $0.0210/GB-Mo -> matches FALLBACK_AURORA_BACKUP_GB_MONTH=0.021 and the Aurora cluster-snapshot rate. The two usagetype substrings ('ChargedBackupUsage' / 'Aurora:BackupUsage') exactly match the CE reconciliation keys in services/advisor.py:89-92, so reconcile_snapshot_savings caps the correct pool. (3) gp2 vs gp3 base storage: productFamily=Database Storage, Single-AZ, volumeType General Purpose (gp2) = $0.1150/GB-Mo AND General Purpose-GP3 (gp3) = $0.1150/GB-Mo across every engine row -> confirms the documented gp2==gp3 assumption STILL HOLDS, so the deliberate absence of a gp2->gp3 RDS check is correct (no missed savings). Instance/edition/license/deployment and Aurora storage-mode SKUs are deterministically pinned via TERM_MATCH filters (pricing_engine.py:1163-1190) and _extract_usd reads only the OnDemand term, so no MaxResults=1 nondeterminism on the instance path; a specific instance-class price was not individually re-derived (best-effort, filters confirmed correct). Region scaling verified single-applied: services/rds.py _rds_monthly_price and snapshot paths call PricingEngine directly with no extra pricing_multiplier; multiplier appears only on fallback constants (pricing_engine.py:576,630-635,661).

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
|---|---|---|---|
| Compute Optimizer rightsizing | counted | compute-optimizer get_rds_database_recommendations returns rdsDBRecommendations with compute_optimizer_savings>0 (services/advisor.py:256-265) | savingsOpportunity.estimatedMonthlySavings.value summed across instance/storage option arrays (services/_savings.py:46-69) |
| Cost Optimization Hub rightsizing/idle/storage (RdsDbInstance + RdsDbCluster) | counted | ctx.cost_hub_splits['rds'] from RdsDbInstance/RdsDbCluster currentResourceType (scan_orchestrator.py:90-91), filtered by _coh_is_renderable (rds.py:22-36,111-113) | estimatedMonthlySavings flat float summed (rds_logic.py:249) |
| Multi-AZ Optimization (disable in non-prod) | counted | MultiAZ=True AND non-prod (Environment tag or name substring) AND CloudWatch DatabaseConnections avg<=20 over 14d (services/rds.py:394-444) | exact delta multi_az_price - single_az_price via live get_rds_instance_monthly_price (services/rds.py:447-456) |
| Non-Production Scheduling (stop nights/weekends) | counted | DB name contains dev/test/staging/qa AND engine not Aurora AND CloudWatch DatabaseConnections avg<=1.0 over 14d (services/rds.py:547-561) | live monthly price x fixed 0.65 reduction factor RDS_NON_PROD_SCHEDULE_REDUCTION (services/rds.py:564-568) |
| Old RDS Snapshots | counted | manual snapshot age_days > old_snapshot_days (services/rds.py:668-710) | upper bound AllocatedStorage x backup rate; capped at CE actual per engine pool (services/rds.py:118-142,680-683; rds_logic.py:117-176); 0-size -> advisory no $0.00 |
| Old Aurora Cluster Snapshots | counted | manual cluster snapshot age_days > old_snapshot_days (services/rds.py:727-779) | upper bound AllocatedStorage x Aurora backup rate $0.021 (services/rds.py:735-742) |
| Reserved Instance Opportunities | advisory | DBInstanceStatus available (services/rds.py:609-663) | RI discount matrix (0.38-0.62) x live price; Counted=False, ADVISORY_CATEGORIES, excluded from total (rds_logic.py:23-25,251) |
| Backup Retention Optimization | advisory | BackupRetentionPeriod > 7 (services/rds.py:490-536) | no $ figure (free allotment=100% of provisioned; not derivable at scan time); excluded from total |

**Findings:**

#### 🟠 H1 · Aurora provisioned instance double-counted across the RDS tab and the Aurora tab (no cross-adapter dedup)  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/rds.py:107-127`
- **Evidence:** Orchestrator buckets BOTH RdsDbInstance and RdsDbCluster Cost-Hub recs into the 'rds' split (core/scan_orchestrator.py:90-91), and the RDS Compute Optimizer call get_rds_database_recommendations (services/advisor.py:260-265) also returns Aurora DB-instance recs. These are summed into the RDS total via resolve_rds_findings (services/rds_logic.py:246-251). The aurora adapter independently rightsizes/Graviton-migrates the SAME provisioned Aurora member instances and sums them into the Aurora total (services/adapters/aurora.py:181-277,459-465). resolve_rds_findings dedups ONLY within rds sources; there is no covered-set spanning rds<->aurora, and core/result_builder.py:72 sums f.total_monthly_savings across ALL services with no cross-tab dedup.
- **Impact:** Inflated account-wide headline: the same Aurora instance's rightsizing dollars are added in both the RDS and Aurora per-tab totals and again in summary.total_monthly_savings. Magnitude scales with provisioned Aurora instances that CO/CoH also surface.
- **Fix:** Establish a single owner for provisioned-Aurora-instance rightsizing: either have aurora.py skip instances whose normalized id appears in ctx.cost_hub_splits['rds']/RDS CO output, or exclude aurora-engine instances from RDS CO/CoH counting; record suppressed ids in a shared covered set. Add a regression test with one Aurora instance present in both CO and aurora rightsizing.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** All cited code verified. scan_orchestrator.py:90-91 buckets BOTH RdsDbInstance and RdsDbCluster into the 'rds' CoH split (no 'aurora' bucket exists), so Aurora member instances/clusters flow into ctx.cost_hub_splits['rds']. advisor.py:260-265 (get_rds_database_recommendations, RDS CO surface that covers Aurora DB instances) and rds.py:111-127 feed CO+CoH into resolve_rds_findings, which sums them into the RDS total at rds_logic.py:246-251. resolve_rds_findings dedups ONLY within RDS sources: coh_keys (line 216) is built solely from the RDS CoH split and the best-per-key winner only ranks RDS CO/heuristic recs — there is no covered-set spanning rds<->aurora. Independently, aurora.py:148-277 (_check_provisioned_instances) directly enumerates describe_db_instances, filters engine.startswith('aurora') (line 183), and emits instance_rightsizing/instance_graviton recs for the SAME provisioned member instances, summed into the Aurora total at aurora.py:457-465. The Aurora adapter never reads cost_hub_splits or any RDS covered-set (grep confirmed zero references) — the two adapters are mutually blind. result_builder.py:72 then sums every tab's total_monthly_savings into summary.total_monthly_savings with no cross-tab dedup. The design defect (no cross-adapter dedup; Aurora-inclusive RDS recs and Aurora-adapter rightsizing both fold into the account headline) is fully demonstrated in code; the only non-code dependency is whether a live account's CO/CoH actually surface a given over-provisioned Aurora member instance that the Aurora adapter also flags, which AWS Compute Optimizer/Cost Optimization Hub do for supported Aurora engines, so the headline double-count materializes for any such instance. Severity HIGH is appropriate (inflated primary account-wide number); magnitude scales with over-provisioned provisioned (non-serverless) Aurora instances surfaced by both paths. Minor framing nuance: the two per-tab totals are each correct for their own tab; the actual dollar inflation is the cross-tab sum at result_builder.py:72, which the finding correctly identifies.

#### 🟡 M1 · Non-prod scheduling saving uses a fixed 0.65 reduction factor (counted), not a schedule-derived delta  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/rds.py:68, 564-568`
- **Evidence:** RDS_NON_PROD_SCHEDULE_REDUCTION=0.65 (services/rds.py:68) is applied as sched_savings = sched_base_price * 0.65 (line 568) and lands in the COUNTED concrete bucket (rds_logic.py:230-234,246). The 0.65 is a static estimate of nights+weekends-off, not the user's actual schedule, though gated on genuine idle evidence (avg DatabaseConnections<=1.0 over 14d, services/rds.py:557-561).
- **Impact:** Counted headline can over/understate this lever if realized downtime differs from ~65%. Bounded by the idle gate; per-DB error rather than systemic.
- **Fix:** Keep the idle gate but present scheduling as a range or clearly label 0.65 as a planning factor (AuditBasis formula already notes it); optionally demote to advisory unless a configured schedule is known. Acceptable as a documented tradeoff if retained.

#### 🟢 L1 · Backup-retention advisory always prices at the standard rate, ignoring Aurora engine  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/rds.py:490-495`
- **Evidence:** backup_price = ctx.pricing_engine.get_rds_backup_storage_price_per_gb() is called with NO engine argument (services/rds.py:491-492), so the advisory text/AuditBasis always show $0.095/GB-mo even for an Aurora DB whose true rate is $0.021/GB-mo (validated live). Contrast services/rds.py:106-115 _backup_rate which passes the engine for snapshots.
- **Impact:** Cosmetic only: this category is advisory (no $ summed into headline), so no dollar leakage. The displayed per-GB rate is ~4.5x too high for Aurora DBs.
- **Fix:** Pass the instance engine: get_rds_backup_storage_price_per_gb(engine), mirroring the snapshot path.

#### 🟢 L2 · Scheduling check gated on DB-name substring only; ignores the Environment tag the Multi-AZ check honors  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/rds.py:547-551`
- **Evidence:** Non-prod scheduling only fires when the DB identifier literally contains dev/test/staging/qa (services/rds.py:547). The Multi-AZ check first reads the Environment/Stage/Env tag and only falls back to the name substring (services/rds.py:401-435). A non-prod DB tagged Environment=staging but named e.g. 'billing-db' is eligible for Multi-AZ-disable but NOT for scheduling despite identical idle evidence.
- **Impact:** Coverage gap / missed savings on tag-classified non-prod DBs whose name lacks the keywords; inconsistent classification between the two levers.
- **Fix:** Reuse the tag-aware non-prod resolution (lines 401-435) for the scheduling gate instead of the standalone name-substring test at line 547.

#### 🟢 L3 · Multi-AZ-disable check lacks the Aurora-engine exclusion that scheduling has  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/rds.py:394-456`
- **Evidence:** The scheduling check excludes Aurora (schedulable_engine = bool(engine) and not engine.startswith('aurora'), services/rds.py:556), but the Multi-AZ block (services/rds.py:394-456) has no such guard. For an Aurora member instance reporting MultiAZ=True it would price single/Multi-AZ via standard RDS deploymentOption SKUs that do not represent Aurora HA, and would also feed the H1 cross-tab overlap.
- **Impact:** Low likelihood (Aurora members rarely report instance-level MultiAZ=True), but if triggered it mis-prices and compounds the H1 double-count.
- **Fix:** Add `and not (engine or '').startswith('aurora')` to the Multi-AZ trigger so Aurora HA is left to the aurora adapter.

---

### Redshift — `services/adapters/redshift.py`

**Module identity:** key="redshift", cli_aliases=("redshift",), display_name="Redshift", required_clients()=("redshift",) — OMITS "redshift-serverless" though the shim calls ctx.client("redshift-serverless") (services/redshift.py:82). No requires_cloudwatch / reads_fast_mode declared, and the path reads NO CloudWatch — every saving is config-derived with zero usage evidence. Emits ONE source block: "enhanced_checks" (services/adapters/redshift.py:75). No cost_optimization_hub block and no Compute Optimizer (CO does not cover Redshift). Adapter docstring says "Flat-rate adapter for Redshift" / "Flat-rate savings strategy" (redshift.py:1,25) yet it calls the LIVE Pricing API ctx.pricing_engine.get_instance_monthly_price("AmazonRedshift", node_type) (redshift.py:68). NOTE on required_clients: grep shows it is referenced only in tests (tests/test_s3_adapter.py) and base/contract definitions — no orchestrator/CLI consumer gates scanning on it, so omitting redshift-serverless does NOT block the client (ctx.client creates it on demand); the contract is simply inaccurate. CLAUDE.md drift: services/adapters/CLAUDE.md Live-Pricing table (19 adapters) does NOT list redshift.py at all, and there is no Flat-rate row for it either — the adapter is a live-priced adapter missing from the doc and mislabeled "flat-rate" in its own docstring.

**Verdict:** Redshift is a single-source, live-priced adapter (source block 'enhanced_checks') that renders via the generic per-rec path (no PHASE_B handler; not in _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC). Two CRITICAL confirmed bugs dominate. (C1) The orchestrator populates ctx.cost_hub_splits['redshift'] from RedshiftCluster but RedshiftModule.scan never reads it (grep: zero references) — real Cost-Hub cluster savings are silently dropped, the orphaned-bucket class flagged in the brief. (C2) The node price comes from get_instance_monthly_price -> _fetch_generic_instance_price, which filters only instanceType+location with MaxResults=1 and no unit/productFamily guard; the live Pricing API shows 3-4 OnDemand SKUs per node type (Concurrency Scaling $/sec, Managed Storage $/GB-Mo, Free Usage $0, and the wanted Compute Instance $/hr) with unstable ordering across node types (Compute Instance is returned LAST for ra3.4xlarge, FIRST for dc2.large) — so the counted node price is non-deterministic and usually the wrong dimension (e.g. $0.66/mo vs the correct $2,379.80/mo for ra3.4xlarge). Crucially, contrary to the brief's hypothesis, Cluster Rightsizing and Serverless count $0 because their rec dicts lack a 'NodeType' key (the `if node_type:` guard skips them), so there is NO RI+rightsizing dollar stack — the ONLY counted dollar in the whole tab is the RI heuristic at factor 0.52, which (H1) should be demoted to advisory like RDS/commitment_analysis, (H2) disagrees with its own card string ('$nodes*150') and '24%' text and overstates a 1-yr RI by ~2x, and (H3) is rendered as a hardcoded string while the tab sums a different live-priced number (counted != rendered). The $0 rightsizing (M1) and serverless (M2) recs are not marked Counted=False, so they inflate total_recommendations and the 'counted' tally with placeholder dollar cards. Serverless errors are swallowed by a bare except: pass (M3). RA3 managed storage is unpriced (M4, TODO confirmed at $0.024/GB-Mo). Lower-severity: config-only savings with no usage evidence (L1), dead fallback constant/pause factor/empty buckets (L2), string-timestamp age=30 mis-gate (L3), and 'Resource' card titles (L4). Pricing validated live (us-east-1, 2026-06-25): ra3.4xlarge Compute Node $3.26/hr->$2,379.80/mo, dc2.large $0.25/hr->$182.50/mo, RMS $0.024/GB-Mo. Net: after fixing C2/H1, the correct counted Redshift tab total is ~$0 until CoH (C1) is wired in with CoH>heuristic cluster-id dedup.

**Pricing validation:** Validated live against AWS Pricing API (AmazonRedshift, us-east-1, OnDemand), 2026-06-25 price version. ra3.4xlarge returns FOUR OnDemand SKUs matching instanceType+location: (1) Redshift Concurrency Scaling usagetype CS:ra3.4xlarge = $0.0009/Node-second [returned FIRST], (2) Redshift Managed Storage RMS:ra3.4xlarge = $0.024/GB-Mo, (3) Concurrency Scaling Free Usage = $0.00/second, (4) Compute Instance usagetype Node:ra3.4xlarge = $3.26/Compute Node-hour [returned LAST] -> correct node price = $3.26 x 730 = $2,379.80/mo. dc2.large returns THREE OnDemand SKUs: Compute Instance Node:dc2.large = $0.25/hr [returned FIRST] -> $182.50/mo, plus two Concurrency Scaling rows ($0.00 and $0.00007/second). The Compute Instance SKU's position is FIRST for dc2.large but LAST for ra3.4xlarge — proving ordering is not stable across node types, so the adapter's MaxResults=1 + instanceType/location-only filter is non-deterministic. RMS $0.024/GB-Mo confirmed (matches the in-code TODO). RI factor 0.52: real 1-year Redshift reserved-node discount is ~20-33% (No/Partial/All Upfront); 3-year up to ~75%. The shim text/strings advertise '24%' (a ~1-yr figure) while the adapter counts 52% — overstating a '1-year RI' saving by ~2x.

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
|---|---|---|---|
| Reserved Instance Optimization (reserved_instances bucket) | counted | ClusterStatus=='available' AND ClusterCreateTime present AND NumberOfNodes>=2 AND cluster_age_days>30 (services/redshift.py:46-68) | COUNTED: get_instance_monthly_price('AmazonRedshift', NodeType) x NumberOfNodes x 0.52 (adapters/redshift.py:53-54,68-70). Rec carries NodeType+NumberOfNodes so it is the ONLY check that produces a non-zero counted dollar. Rendered card instead shows hardcoded string '${nodes*150}/month with 1-year RI' and text '24% savings'. |
| Cluster Rightsizing (cluster_rightsizing bucket) | counted | NumberOfNodes>3 (services/redshift.py:70) | EFFECTIVELY $0 COUNTED: rec dict has NO 'NodeType' key (and uses 'CurrentNodes', not 'NumberOfNodes'), so adapter guard `if node_type:` is False -> contributes $0 (adapters/redshift.py:62-70). Card still renders the string '${(nodes-2)*100}/month potential'. Not marked Counted=False, so it inflates total_recommendations and the 'counted' header tally. |
| Serverless Optimization (serverless_optimization bucket) | counted | redshift-serverless workgroup status=='AVAILABLE' (services/redshift.py:91) | $0 COUNTED: rec has no 'NodeType' -> `if node_type:` False -> $0 (adapters/redshift.py:65). Card renders '$150/month with reservations'. Not marked Counted=False. |
| pause_resume_scheduling bucket | advisory | Declared in checks dict (services/redshift.py:30) but NEVER populated — no paused/idle cluster detection exists | Dead branch. The REDSHIFT_SAVINGS_FACTORS['pause']=1.00 factor and the _rs_factor pause/unused/inactive mapping (adapters/redshift.py:55-56) therefore never fire. |
| storage_optimization bucket | advisory | Declared (services/redshift.py:31) but NEVER populated — no RA3 managed-storage check exists | Dead branch (the adapter has only an in-code TODO at redshift.py:47-48). |

**Findings:**

#### 🔴 C1 · Orphaned Cost-Hub bucket: ctx.cost_hub_splits['redshift'] populated by orchestrator but never consumed by the adapter  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/redshift.py:35-83`
- **Evidence:** scan_orchestrator buckets RedshiftCluster -> 'redshift' (core/scan_orchestrator.py:94) and 'redshift' is in _HUB_SERVICES (scan_orchestrator.py:59), so ctx.cost_hub_splits['redshift'] is filled with real CoH cluster recommendations. grep confirms the adapter AND services/redshift.py never reference cost_hub_splits at all (only matches are the dead REDSHIFT_NODE_MONTHLY_FALLBACK). RedshiftModule.scan reads only get_enhanced_redshift_checks.
- **Impact:** Real, AWS-computed CoH cluster savings (the highest-authority source) are silently dropped from the Redshift tab — pure savings leakage. No CoH<->heuristic dedup exists because CoH is never read.
- **Fix:** In scan(), read recs = ctx.cost_hub_splits.get('redshift', []) (mirror services/rds_logic.py), sum estimatedMonthlySavings via services/_savings.compute_optimizer_savings/CoH float, emit a 'cost_optimization_hub' SourceBlock, and dedup CoH > heuristic by normalized cluster id so a cluster surfaced by both CoH and the heuristic is counted once.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** scan_orchestrator.py maps RedshiftCluster->'redshift' (line 94) and 'redshift' is in _HUB_SERVICES (line 59), so ctx.cost_hub_splits['redshift'] is populated with real CoH cluster recommendations. grep over services/ confirms neither services/adapters/redshift.py nor services/redshift.py reference cost_hub_splits at all (the consuming adapters are ec2/ebs/rds/lambda_svc/dynamodb/containers/eks/commitment_analysis). RedshiftModule.scan reads only get_enhanced_redshift_checks(ctx) (adapters/redshift.py:49). The cluster-level CoH recs land in an unconsumed bucket and are dropped. Note RedshiftReservedInstances CoH recs are separately routed to commitment_analysis (line 108), but RedshiftCluster rightsizing/idle recs have no other sink. Savings leakage confirmed.

#### 🔴 C2 · Non-deterministic node-price SKU lookup (MaxResults=1; 3-4 SKUs share instanceType) corrupts the only counted dollar figure  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `core/pricing_engine.py:1290-1298, 1590-1622`
- **Evidence:** _fetch_generic_instance_price filters ONLY on instanceType+location (1291-1294); _call_pricing_api uses MaxResults=1 and returns _extract_usd(PriceList[0]) with NO unit/productFamily check (1598-1613). Live API proof: ra3.4xlarge matches 4 OnDemand SKUs with Concurrency Scaling ($0.0009/sec) returned FIRST and Compute Instance ($3.26/hr) LAST; dc2.large matches 3 with Compute Instance FIRST. _extract_usd would return $0.0009 -> x730 = $0.66/mo for ra3 instead of the correct $3.26 x 730 = $2,379.80/mo (off ~3,600x); if the RMS row ($0.024/GB-Mo) is picked it yields $17.52; if the CSFreeUsage $0 row is picked, get_instance_monthly_price returns 0.0 and the finding is silently dropped by the `if monthly>0` guard.
- **Impact:** The RI heuristic (the sole counted dollar in the entire Redshift tab) is multiplied by a node price that is usually the wrong pricing dimension and unstable across node types — the counted savings are effectively garbage (near-zero or a per-GB/per-second rate mis-counted as a node-hour).
- **Fix:** Pin the SKU deterministically: add filters productFamily='Compute Instance' (and/or usagetype LIKE 'Node:'+instance_type), fetch MaxResults>1, and select the row whose price unit is 'Hrs' (mirror the _call_pricing_api_hourly / _select_efs_storage_rate unit-guard patterns already in this file). Reject Concurrency Scaling / Managed Storage / Free Usage rows.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Verified mechanism in code AND empirically via live AWS Pricing API. _fetch_generic_instance_price filters only instanceType+location (pricing_engine.py:1291-1294); _call_pricing_api uses MaxResults=1 (1601), no productFamily/usagetype/unit filter, returns _extract_usd(PriceList[0]) (1611); adapter calls get_instance_monthly_price('AmazonRedshift', node_type) (adapters/redshift.py:68). Live query for ra3.4xlarge+US East (N. Virginia) returned 4 OnDemand SKUs all carrying instanceType=ra3.4xlarge: Redshift Concurrency Scaling $0.0009/sec, Redshift Managed Storage $0.024/GB-Mo, CSFreeUsage $0.00/sec, and Compute Instance $3.26/Hr. Math confirmed: correct $3.26*730=$2,379.80; CS $0.0009*730=$0.66 (~3,622x low); RMS $0.024*730=$17.52; CSFreeUsage $0 -> _extract_usd returns None (value>0 guard, line 1633) -> 0.0 fallback -> dropped by 'if monthly>0'. In this response Compute Instance was ordered LAST, so a MaxResults=1 fetch would NOT get the correct node-hour price. Non-deterministic wrong-dimension pricing of the sole counted dollar is real.

#### 🟠 H1 · RI heuristic is Counted=True (only counted lever) instead of advisory — double-counts the commitment lever  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/redshift.py:51-70`
- **Evidence:** _rs_factor maps CheckCategory 'Reserved Instance Optimization' -> 0.52 and the adapter adds monthly*nodes*0.52 to total_monthly_savings (53-54,68-70). RDS demotes the equivalent to ADVISORY_CATEGORIES / Counted=False (services/rds_logic.py:23-25,79) and the orchestrator already routes RedshiftReservedInstances CoH recs to commitment_analysis (scan_orchestrator.py:108). No rec in this adapter ever sets Counted=False (grep: zero 'Counted' occurrences).
- **Impact:** Counts a Reserved-Instance buy (a commitment lever, no usage evidence) as account savings on the Redshift tab, overlapping the commitment_analysis RI view. Because rightsizing/serverless count $0 (see M1/M2), this RI number IS the Redshift tab total — demoting it correctly drops the counted tab total to $0 until CoH is wired (C1).
- **Fix:** Tag the RI rec Counted=False (add an ADVISORY_CATEGORIES set mirroring rds_logic) so it renders but is excluded from total_monthly_savings; let commitment_analysis own the RI dollars.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** adapters/redshift.py adds savings unconditionally: savings += monthly * num_nodes * factor with factor 0.52 for 'reserved' (lines 54,70), feeding ServiceFindings.total_monthly_savings (80). No Counted=False anywhere in the adapter or services/redshift.py. RDS demotes its RI equivalent via ADVISORY_CATEGORIES (rds_logic.py:23-25), and scan_orchestrator routes RedshiftReservedInstances CoH recs to commitment_analysis (line 108), so the Redshift tab counting an RI commitment lever overlaps the commitment view. The RI heuristic being Counted=True instead of advisory is confirmed.

#### 🟠 H2 · RI saving: three disagreeing numbers (string $nodes*150 vs text '24%' vs counted 0.52) and ~2x overstatement  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/redshift.py:17, 60-64`
- **Evidence:** Shim sets EstimatedSavings=f'${number_of_nodes*150:.2f}/month with 1-year RI' (64), Recommendation text '...24% savings potential' (62-63), and REDSHIFT_OPTIMIZATION_DESCRIPTIONS says 'up to 24%' (17); the adapter instead counts node_price*nodes*0.52 (adapters/redshift.py:53-54). Live validation: 1-yr Redshift reserved-node discount ~20-33%, so 0.52 (52%) overstates a '1-year RI' by ~2x.
- **Impact:** Headline counted number disagrees with both the rendered card string and the stated '24%' rationale; the 52% factor materially overstates the realizable 1-yr RI discount.
- **Fix:** Pick one source of truth: if RI stays counted, use a defensible 1-yr factor (~0.30) or the exact RI vs on-demand delta from the Pricing API, and write that priced figure into EstimatedSavings so the card matches the tab. Per H1, prefer making it advisory.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** Three disagreeing figures verified: EstimatedSavings string f'${number_of_nodes*150:.2f}/month with 1-year RI' (services/redshift.py:64), Recommendation text '24% savings potential' (62-63), REDSHIFT_OPTIMIZATION_DESCRIPTIONS 'up to 24%' (17), while the adapter counts node_price*nodes*0.52 (adapters/redshift.py:54,70). Overstatement substantiated by live RI pricing for ra3.4xlarge: 1yr No-Upfront $2.282/hr (~30% off $3.26), 1yr Partial-Upfront effective ~$2.18/hr (~33% off); 52% actually corresponds to ~3yr discounts (~56-62%). For the explicitly-stated '1-year RI' the 0.52 factor overstates realizable discount by ~1.6-1.7x. The finding's '~2x' is a mild but acceptable approximation; core inconsistency claim is fully correct.

#### 🟠 H3 · Counted != rendered: generic renderer shows hardcoded shim strings while the tab total counts a live-priced number  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `reporter_phase_b.py:1874-1875 (with 1380-1381, 2548-2550)`
- **Evidence:** redshift is NOT in PHASE_B_HANDLERS and NOT in _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC, so should_fallback_to_per_rec('redshift')=True and render_generic_per_rec dispatches to _render_generic_other_rec, which prints rec['EstimatedSavings'] verbatim (reporter_phase_b.py:1874-1875). Cards therefore show '${nodes*150}', '${(nodes-2)*100}', '$150' while the tab total = node_price*nodes*0.52 (RI) + $0 + $0. No _RECOMMENDATION_FILTERS['redshift'] exists (html_report_generator.py:453-455) so the desync is purely string-vs-counted.
- **Impact:** Every Redshift card advertises a dollar figure unrelated to (and for RI, ~2x different from) the number summed into the tab/executive headline — counted != rendered.
- **Fix:** Write the adapter's priced per-rec contribution into each rec's EstimatedSavings before emitting the SourceBlock (or add a Redshift PHASE_B handler) so the card string equals the counted figure; emit '$0.00/month - advisory' for the $0 recs.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** redshift is absent from PHASE_B_HANDLERS (reporter_phase_b.py:2436-2498) and from _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC (2516-2530), so should_fallback_to_per_rec('redshift') returns True (2548-2550). render_generic_per_rec's dispatch has no redshift branch, falling to else -> _render_generic_other_rec (1381), which emits rec['EstimatedSavings'] verbatim (1874-1875) — i.e. the shim strings ${nodes*150}, ${(nodes-2)*100}, $150. Meanwhile the tab total counts node_price*nodes*0.52 (+$0 rightsizing/serverless). _RECOMMENDATION_FILTERS has only 'ec2' (html_report_generator.py:453-455), no 'redshift'. Counted != rendered confirmed. (redshift appears in should_skip_section_header's set at line 2535, but that only suppresses the section header and does not affect per-rec rendering.)

#### 🟡 M1 · Cluster Rightsizing counts $0 (rec lacks NodeType) yet renders '$(nodes-2)*100' and is not marked advisory; the hypothesized RI+rightsizing stack does NOT occur  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/redshift.py:70-79`
- **Evidence:** The cluster_rightsizing rec dict contains ClusterIdentifier, CurrentNodes, Recommendation, EstimatedSavings, CheckCategory — but NO 'NodeType' and uses 'CurrentNodes' not 'NumberOfNodes' (services/redshift.py:71-78). In the adapter, node_type=rec.get('NodeType') is None -> `if node_type:` False -> contributes $0 (adapters/redshift.py:62-70). It is never tagged Counted=False, so _counted_advisory_counts treats it as 'counted' (html_report_generator.py:382-387) and it inflates total_recommendations. Because rightsizing is $0, the brief's hypothesized 0.76x (0.52+0.24) RI+rightsizing stack on one cluster does NOT actually happen in dollars — only RI is counted.
- **Impact:** A $0 placeholder is shown as a counted recommendation advertising a non-zero '$(nodes-2)*100' card, inflating the counted recommendation tally with no realizable dollars; the real rightsizing lever is never quantified. (If a NodeType were later added, the 0.24-of-whole-cluster factor vs the exact remove-2-nodes delta node_price*2 would then be wrong — prefer current-target.)
- **Fix:** Either (a) mark this rec Counted=False (advisory) since it produces no priced saving, or (b) carry NodeType+NumberOfNodes and compute the exact delta node_price*(CurrentNodes-target) with a usage-gated target, not a flat 0.24 of the whole cluster.

#### 🟡 M2 · Serverless rec: $0 counted but '$150/month' rendered, not marked advisory  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/redshift.py:91-101`
- **Evidence:** Serverless rec has WorkgroupName/Recommendation/EstimatedSavings/CheckCategory but no NodeType, so adapter `if node_type:` is False -> $0 (adapters/redshift.py:65). EstimatedSavings='$150/month with reservations' is rendered by _render_generic_other_rec. No Counted=False flag.
- **Impact:** Card advertises $150 while contributing $0; inflates total_recommendations / counted tally. Redshift Serverless is RPU-priced and is never actually quantified.
- **Fix:** Mark serverless recs Counted=False and set EstimatedSavings to '$0.00/month - advisory (RPU pricing not modeled)', or price RPU-hours from CloudWatch usage.

#### 🟡 M3 · Serverless block swallows all exceptions silently (bare except: pass) — permission gap/throttle vanishes  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/redshift.py:81-103`
- **Evidence:** The redshift-serverless list_workgroups loop is wrapped in `try: ... except Exception: pass` with no ctx.warn / ctx.permission_issue (102-103). The outer cluster block does ctx.warn (105-106). required_clients() omits 'redshift-serverless' (adapters/redshift.py:31-33) though it is not a functional gate (no consumer found), so the client is still created — but an AccessDenied/UnauthorizedOperation/throttle on redshift-serverless:ListWorkgroups is silently discarded.
- **Impact:** A permission or throttling failure on the serverless API produces no warning and no permission_issue — the entire serverless path silently no-ops with no operator signal.
- **Fix:** Replace `except Exception: pass` with classification (mirror services/_aws_errors.record_aws_error): AccessDenied/UnauthorizedOperation/OptInRequired -> ctx.permission_issue, else ctx.warn. Add 'redshift-serverless' to required_clients() for contract accuracy.

#### 🟡 M4 · RA3 managed storage ($0.024/GB-Mo) unpriced — RA3 cost basis materially undercounted  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/redshift.py:47-48`
- **Evidence:** In-code TODO: 'RA3 node types charge managed storage at $0.024/GB/month ... Current calculation only covers instance pricing, not RMS storage.' Live API confirms RMS:ra3.4xlarge = $0.024/GB-Mo. The savings basis uses Compute Instance node-hours only.
- **Impact:** For RA3 clusters, the cost basis (and thus any RI/rightsizing saving derived from it) omits managed storage, undercounting RA3 spend. Paused RA3 clusters still bill RMS but are never flagged.
- **Fix:** When NodeType starts with 'ra3', add RMS = describe-derived storage GB (or DescribeStorage) * $0.024 (region-correct) to the cluster cost basis used for savings.

#### 🟢 L1 · Config-only savings with no usage evidence (no CloudWatch)  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/redshift.py:31-73`
- **Evidence:** Adapter declares no requires_cloudwatch/reads_fast_mode and reads no CloudWatch; the RI gate is age>30d AND nodes>=2 (services/redshift.py:46-53) — neither is a utilization signal. The single counted figure (RI) is derived purely from describe_clusters config.
- **Impact:** The counted Redshift saving is not defensible from utilization evidence; an over-provisioned-but-busy cluster and an idle cluster are treated identically.
- **Fix:** Gate counted rightsizing/RI savings on CPU/query-utilization (declare requires_cloudwatch/reads_fast_mode), and attach a structured AuditBasis (rate/region/node-type/metric-window/formula) to each counted finding.

#### 🟢 L2 · Dead constants and dead branches: REDSHIFT_NODE_MONTHLY_FALLBACK, pause 1.00 factor, default 0.24, two empty buckets  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/redshift.py:11, 17-21, 51-57`
- **Evidence:** grep shows REDSHIFT_NODE_MONTHLY_FALLBACK=200.0 referenced only at its definition (11) and a comment (72) — unused. The 'pause' 1.00 factor and the _rs_factor pause/unused/inactive branch (55-56) never fire (no rec uses those categories). The 'default' 0.24 factor never multiplies anything because both recs mapping to it (rightsizing, serverless) lack NodeType -> $0. Buckets pause_resume_scheduling/storage_optimization (services/redshift.py:30-31) are declared but never populated.
- **Impact:** Misleading dead code; the factor table implies pause/rightsizing dollars that the code never produces.
- **Fix:** Delete REDSHIFT_NODE_MONTHLY_FALLBACK and the unused factor entries/buckets, OR implement a real paused-cluster (ClusterStatus=='paused') RMS check to populate pause_resume_scheduling.

#### 🟢 L3 · ClusterCreateTime string-fallback hardcodes age=30 -> RI gate never fires on that path  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/redshift.py:46-53`
- **Evidence:** When ClusterCreateTime is a str, cluster_age_days=30 (48-49); the gate is `if cluster_age_days > 30` (53), so 30>30 is False -> RI rec is skipped. Cannot over-count (it under-counts that edge case).
- **Impact:** On any code path where the SDK yields a string timestamp, the cluster is permanently excluded from the RI heuristic. Low impact since boto3 normally returns a datetime.
- **Fix:** Parse the ISO string to a datetime (or use ClusterCreateTime directly) instead of hardcoding 30, so the age gate evaluates correctly.

#### 🟢 L4 · Cluster cards titled '... : Resource' — resource_id chain omits ClusterIdentifier  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `reporter_phase_b.py:1815-1861`
- **Evidence:** RI/rightsizing recs key the cluster as 'ClusterIdentifier', but the _render_generic_other_rec resource_id fallback chain checks ClusterName/ClusterArn/WorkgroupName etc. and NOT 'ClusterIdentifier' (1815-1861), so it falls through to the literal 'Resource'. (Serverless recs do resolve via WorkgroupName.)
- **Impact:** Cosmetic: RI and rightsizing cards read 'Reserved Instance Optimization: Resource' with no cluster id, reducing report usefulness. No dollar impact.
- **Fix:** Add `or rec.get('ClusterIdentifier')` to the resource_id chain (or give Redshift a dedicated handler).

### S3 — `services/adapters/s3.py`

**Module identity:** RECONCILED — matches services/adapters/CLAUDE.md s3 row and the brief. services/adapters/s3.py: key="s3" (L32), cli_aliases=("s3",) (L33), display_name="S3" (L34), requires_cloudwatch=True (L38), reads_fast_mode=True (L39), required_clients()→("s3","cloudwatch") (L41-43). Two-source adapter: s3_bucket_analysis (dedicated $ source, evidence-gated) + enhanced_checks (visibility-only $0). Pricing path confirmed: services/s3.py:_s3_price_per_gb (L684-710) uses ctx.pricing_engine.for_region(bucket_region) → get_s3_monthly_price_per_gb (core/pricing_engine.py L668-680); _SC_MAP (L614) maps GLACIER_FLEXIBLE_RETRIEVAL→GLACIER, GLACIER_INSTANT_RETRIEVAL→GLACIER_IR. CLAUDE.md correctly omits any CoH consumption claim for s3 (consistent with the orphan reality). No doc-vs-code identity drift.

**Verdict:** The s3 adapter is in good cost-correctness shape and the prior S3-A..S3-J fixes still hold: savings are evidence-gated (counted only when StandardGB>0 AND request metrics prove 0 GETs/30d AND not fast_mode), priced at the bucket's HOME region via PricingEngine.for_region, summed per storage class at each class's own rate, region-scaled exactly once (pricing_multiplier deliberately del'd), with honest $0 advisories for static-website / no-evidence / fast-mode cases and count hygiene that excludes every $0 record from total_recommendations. Both reporter handlers are registered and fire (s3 in _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC, render_s3_top_tables appended), the headline uses the canonical total_monthly_savings (no render-time recompute/filter for s3), and counted==rendered. The material rate (Standard->Standard-IA $0.0105/GB-mo us-east-1) is validated live and the engine's base-tier selection is confirmed load-bearing. No CRITICAL/HIGH findings. One MEDIUM confirmed bug: CloudWatch metric-read AccessDenied/Throttling is logged at debug only (not ctx.permission_issue/ctx.warn), so a CloudWatch permission gap silently zeroes all S3 sizes/costs/savings (safe direction, but hidden). Four LOW limitations: (N2) live-but-inert Cost Hub orphan — cost_hub_splits['s3'] populated yet consumed by no adapter (AWS emits no S3Bucket CoH recs today, so ~$0 impact, but dead wiring with no drop-warning); (N3) the enhanced-checks renderer's ad-hoc parser would count a per-unit '$/GB' string (latent desync; all enhanced strings are $0 today); (N4) the 'intelligent_tiering' gap class credits buckets that already hold a lifecycle policy (contrary to the brief) while ignoring the IT monitoring fee and IA object-size minimums; (N5) list_buckets is unpaginated (>10k-bucket accounts under-enumerated). Confirmed bug vs limitation are separated above; all are fixable from the cited file+line without re-reading the whole adapter.

**Pricing validation:** VALIDATED live against AWS Pricing API (AmazonS3, us-east-1, publicationDate 2026-06-18). (1) Standard timed storage: SKU WP9ANXZGBYYSGJEA, usagetype TimedStorage-ByteHrs, OnDemand term has 3 tiered priceDimensions and the API serialized $0.022 (next 450 TB, beginRange='51200') BEFORE the $0.023 base tier (beginRange='0') — confirming audit S3-D and proving _extract_s3_base_rate's beginRange=='0' selection (core/pricing_engine.py L1652-1655) is load-bearing and correct; base rate = $0.023/GB-mo, matches S3_STORAGE_COSTS['STANDARD']. (2) Standard-IA: SKU 379GYJUQ5WFBUYGM, usagetype TimedStorage-SIA-ByteHrs, single tier $0.0125/GB-mo, matches S3_STORAGE_COSTS['STANDARD_IA']. Both usagetypes contain 'TimedStorage' and neither has Staging/Overhead, so _select_s3_storage_rate (L1257-1268) selects them correctly; volumeType filters ('Standard', 'Standard - Infrequent Access') match _S3_VOLUME_TYPE_BY_CLASS. (3) Counted delta = 0.023 - 0.0125 = $0.0105/GB-mo, exactly the Standard->Standard-IA delta the scanner credits on StandardGB only. Counted rate is correct; no MaxResults=1 nondeterminism (MaxResults=100 + deterministic base-tier filter).

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
|---|---|---|---|
| s3_bucket_analysis: evidence-gated Standard->Standard-IA delta | counted | opportunity_key in {both_missing, lifecycle_missing, intelligent_tiering} AND StandardGB>0 AND not fast_mode AND _assess_bucket_coldness()=='cold' (0 GET requests over COLD_LOOKBACK_DAYS=30 via whole-bucket request-metrics FilterId) | standard_gb x max(std_rate-ia_rate,0); rates from PricingEngine.for_region(bucket_region).get_s3_monthly_price_per_gb(STANDARD\|STANDARD_IA) (fallback S3_STORAGE_COSTS x S3_REGIONAL_MULTIPLIERS). us-east-1: 0.023-0.0125=$0.0105/GB-mo. EstimatedSavings='$X.XX/month'; PricingBasis recorded. services/s3.py L1044-1062 |
| s3_bucket_analysis: static-website advisory | advisory | opportunity_key=='static_website' (IsStaticWebsite True) | '$0.00/month - data transfer dependent (CloudFront CDN)'; SavingsDelta=0.0 (L1065-1068) |
| s3_bucket_analysis: config-gap, no cold evidence advisory | advisory | has_gap AND (standard_gb>0 OR fast_mode) but coldness != 'cold' (metrics off/denied, or fast-mode sample) | '$0.00/month - enable S3 Storage Class Analysis or request metrics to quantify'; SavingsDelta=0.0, Advisory=True (L1069-1076) |
| s3_bucket_analysis: fully-optimized / other | advisory | opportunity_key=='other' or no Standard bytes | '$0.00/month'; SavingsDelta=0.0 (L1077-1078) |
| enhanced_checks: Incomplete Multipart Uploads | advisory | list_multipart_uploads returns Uploads | '$0.00/month - quantify via S3 Storage Lens (incomplete-upload bytes)' (L1187-1189) |
| enhanced_checks: lifecycle-missing (Storage Class / Static Website Optimization) | advisory | NoSuchLifecycleConfiguration; category 'Static Website Optimization' if static else 'Storage Class Optimization' | '$0.00/month - covered by S3 Bucket Analysis source'; BOTH categories filtered out of counted other_recs by _DEDICATED_CATEGORIES (adapter L23-26,71-74) |
| enhanced_checks: Versioning Optimization | advisory | get_bucket_versioning Status=='Enabled' | '$0.00/month - quantify via S3 Storage Lens (noncurrent-version bytes)' (L1244-1246) |
