### WorkSpaces — `services/adapters/workspaces.py`

**Module identity:** key="workspaces", cli_aliases=("workspaces",), display_name="WorkSpaces", required_clients()=("workspaces",) only — NO cloudwatch client, NO requires_cloudwatch, NO reads_fast_mode (services/adapters/workspaces.py:24-30). Module constant _AUTOSTOP_SAVINGS_FACTOR=0.30 (line 18). Delegates discovery to services/workspaces.py:get_enhanced_workspaces_checks(ctx) (a free function, not a ServiceModule), then re-prices via the hardcoded WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY table (services/workspaces.py:29-37). Emits a single SourceBlock "enhanced_checks" (flattened recommendations). Consumes neither Cost Optimization Hub nor Compute Optimizer (not in scan_orchestrator _HUB_SERVICES). Identity matches services/adapters/CLAUDE.md EXCEPT the Live-Pricing table row, which wrongly lists the pricing method as get_instance_monthly_price("AmazonWorkSpaces", ...) — that method is structurally dead (see pricing_validation).

**Verdict:** WorkSpaces is a config-only adapter (services/adapters/workspaces.py -> services/workspaces.py:get_enhanced_workspaces_checks) with a hardcoded us-east-1 Windows+Included price table (WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY) and NO usage telemetry (required_clients=(\"workspaces\",) only). It emits one SourceBlock 'enhanced_checks' rendered via the generic Phase B per-rec fallback (resource id from rec.get(\"WorkspaceId\"), reporter_phase_b.py:1852) — confirmed it is NOT in _PHASE_A_SERVICES, PHASE_B_HANDLERS, or _PHASE_B_SKIP_PER_REC, so cards do render (no blank/dropped tab). Pagination is full (get_paginator). No Cost Hub / Compute Optimizer (correctly out of scope). Three checks, all counted, none advisory. Confirmed bugs: C1 permission errors swallowed as ctx.warn instead of ctx.permission_issue (tab vanishes on AccessDenied); C2 AutoStop savings fabricated from a flat 0.30 with no login metric (live AutoStop = $19/mo + $0.68/hr, break-even ~87 hrs/mo, wrong-signed for heavy users); C3 billing_mode & unused recs carry no ComputeType so scan() always defaults to STANDARD and counts a fixed $10.50 regardless of real bundle; C4 cards show fabricated '$50/month' and 'Full workspace monthly cost' while headline counts $10.50 (display-vs-counted desync); C5 STOPPED+AUTO_STOP WorkSpaces flagged 'Full workspace monthly cost' though already near-free; C6 one AVAILABLE+ALWAYS_ON over-ranked WorkSpace double-counted across billing_mode + bundle_rightsizing; C7 PowerPro/GraphicsPro constants understated 11%/26% vs live API; M1 rightsizing target arbitrarily gated on ctx.pricing_engine truthiness plus dead `else None`; M2 'utilization profile' claim with no metric. Limitations: L1 Windows+Included-only table ignores BYOL/Linux/storage; L2 CLAUDE.md lists a dead get_instance_monthly_price method. Fix plan: C1 route via record_aws_error; C2 CloudWatch-gate or $0 advisory; C3 propagate real ComputeTypeName; C4 sync display string to counted delta; C5 branch on RunningMode; C6 single-lever dedup; C7 refresh constants w/ AuditBasis; M1 decouple target from engine + delete dead code; M2 reword/gate; L1 key on OS/license; L2 correct the doc row.

**Pricing validation:** Validated live against AWS Pricing API (AmazonWorkSpaces, us-east-1, OnDemand) on 2026-06-27. (1) NO instanceType attribute — get_pricing_service_attributes returns bundle/runningMode/license/operatingSystem/pricingUnit/memory/vcpu/storage/rootvolume/uservolume/softwareIncluded, confirming get_instance_monthly_price(\"AmazonWorkSpaces\",...) is structurally dead and the CLAUDE.md row is wrong (finding L2). A single bundle+AlwaysOn+Included+Windows filter returns many commingled rows ($0 'Basic utilities', WorkSpaces Core, and software add-ons e.g. Office 2021 $21.43 / Visual Studio 2022 Pro $48.51 / Project 2021 $38.01), so a naive first-row lookup would be non-deterministic — justifying a hardcoded table but requiring manual maintenance. (2) Stale constants confirmed (finding C7): PowerPro full bundle live = $140.00/Month (SKU 9M7TNDXEHK432522) vs table 124.0 (-11.4%); GraphicsPro live = $999.00/Month (SKU 4GQGYJZHP5W278AE) vs table 735.0 (-26.4%); GraphicsPro.g4dn = $959 (SKU SAXMZ7UAX736ARQ5). (3) AutoStop structure confirmed (finding C2): Power AutoStop = $19/mo fixed (SKU YE55FXMUCR7VAU2K) + $0.68/hr (SKU XMVTCHAM8XRX95HZ); vs ~$80 AlwaysOn this gives break-even ~87 login-hrs/mo, so the flat _AUTOSTOP_SAVINGS_FACTOR=0.30 is a fabricated midpoint that is wrong-signed for heavy users. NOT validated live this run: VALUE(25)/STANDARD(35)/PERFORMANCE(60)/POWER(80)/GRAPHICS(350) constants — STANDARD is especially load-bearing because finding C3 shows every billing_mode/unused count effectively prices STANDARD; flag for follow-up live validation.

**Cost checks:**

| Check | Status | Trigger | Savings basis |
|---|---|---|---|
| billing_mode_optimization | counted | State=="AVAILABLE" AND WorkspaceProperties.RunningMode=="ALWAYS_ON" (services/workspaces.py:96) | Display string hardcoded "$50/month potential per workspace" (no EstimatedSavingsAmount). Counted by scan() fallback: WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY[compute_type]*pricing_multiplier*0.30. BUT the rec carries NO ComputeType/WorkspaceProperties key, so scan() defaults compute_type to "STANDARD" => always 35*mult*0.30 = $10.50 (at mult=1), bundle-blind. Card $50 vs counted $10.50 desync; factor 0.30 fabricated (no login metric). |
| unused_workspaces | counted | State in {STOPPED, ERROR, SUSPENDED} (services/workspaces.py:110) | Display string "Full workspace monthly cost" (no EstimatedSavingsAmount). Counted by scan() fallback: again defaults compute_type to "STANDARD" (rec has no ComputeType) => 35*mult*0.30 = $10.50, NOT full cost. False positive on STOPPED+AUTO_STOP WorkSpaces (already bill only ~$19/mo fixed). |
| bundle_rightsizing | counted | State=="AVAILABLE" AND WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_RANK[compute_type]>=3; rank>=4 -> target STANDARD only if ctx.pricing_engine truthy, else rank>=3 -> target PERFORMANCE (services/workspaces.py:122-141) | EstimatedSavingsAmount = max(current_price - target_price, 0) where both = WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY[type]*pricing_multiplier (single region scale). Counted directly by scan(). Display string "${savings:.2f}/month" matches counted. Claims "based on utilization profile" but reads no metric. VALUE/STANDARD/PERFORMANCE never rightsized. |

**Findings:**

#### 🟠 C1 · describe_workspaces permission errors swallowed as generic ctx.warn, never classified as permission_issue  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:84-159`
- **Evidence:** Single broad `try:` around the whole pagination loop ends with `except Exception as e: ctx.warn(f"Could not analyze WorkSpaces resources: {e}", "workspaces")` (lines 158-159). No use of services/_aws_errors.record_aws_error, which exists and routes AccessDenied/AccessDeniedException/UnauthorizedOperation/OptInRequired -> ctx.permission_issue (used by services/adapters/network.py:64 and services/rds.py:272). ctx.permission_issue exists (core/scan_context.py:59).
- **Impact:** On an IAM gap (workspaces:DescribeWorkspaces denied) the entire WorkSpaces tab silently degrades to a generic warning and disappears from the report with no permission signal — the operator cannot tell 'no WorkSpaces' from 'no permission'. Mirrors the EC2/RDS anti-pattern the catalogue flags.
- **Fix:** Replace the bare ctx.warn in the except with services._aws_errors.record_aws_error(ctx, e, service="workspaces", context="describe_workspaces failed") so permission codes route to ctx.permission_issue.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** services/workspaces.py:84 opens one broad try: around the entire describe_workspaces paginator loop, ending at lines 158-159 with `except Exception as e: ctx.warn(f"Could not analyze WorkSpaces resources: {e}", "workspaces")`. No import or call of services/_aws_errors.record_aws_error anywhere in the file. record_aws_error exists (services/_aws_errors.py:47-56) and routes AccessDenied/AccessDeniedException/UnauthorizedOperation/OptInRequired (plus SubscriptionRequiredException/AuthFailure) to ctx.permission_issue; ctx.permission_issue exists (core/scan_context.py:59-68) and is the established pattern in services/adapters/network.py:64 and services/rds.py:270-276. So on a workspaces:DescribeWorkspaces IAM gap the failure is mis-classified as a generic warning instead of a permission_issue and never reaches the report's permission-gap signal. One nuance (already acknowledged in the finding): it is not fully silent — a ctx.warn is emitted — but the permission classification is lost, exactly the H4/_aws_errors anti-pattern. HIGH is defensible by the codebase's own standard.

#### 🟠 C2 · AutoStop saving fabricated from a flat 0.30 factor with no login/usage metric  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/workspaces.py:15-18,62-66`
- **Evidence:** _AUTOSTOP_SAVINGS_FACTOR=0.30 (line 18) multiplied into every ALWAYS_ON and unused finding (line 65: bundle_monthly*ctx.pricing_multiplier*0.30). required_clients() returns ("workspaces",) only — no CloudWatch, no metric read anywhere. Live Pricing API (us-east-1): Power AutoStop = $19/mo fixed + $0.68/hr (SKUs YE55FXMUCR7VAU2K + XMVTCHAM8XRX95HZ) vs Power AlwaysOn ~$80/mo => break-even ~87 login-hrs/mo. A light user (20 hrs) saves ~59%; a heavy user (160 hrs) PAYS ~$48 MORE (negative saving) while the scanner still credits +30%.
- **Impact:** Every AutoStop/unused dollar is a config-derived guess that can be wildly wrong and even wrong-signed; it is not defensible from the report. This is the canonical 'config dimension alone -> fabricated $' issue.
- **Fix:** CloudWatch-gate on AWS/WorkSpaces UserConnected/ConnectionAttempt session hours (declare requires_cloudwatch/reads_fast_mode) and compute saving = AlwaysOn - (AutoStop monthly fee + hourly*measured_hours); if no metric, demote to $0 advisory (Counted=False) like lambda_svc / file_systems.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** services/adapters/workspaces.py:18 defines _AUTOSTOP_SAVINGS_FACTOR=0.30; line 65 (else branch) computes savings += bundle_monthly * ctx.pricing_multiplier * 0.30 for every rec lacking EstimatedSavingsAmount — i.e. all billing_mode_optimization (ALWAYS_ON) and unused recs (only bundle_rightsizing sets EstimatedSavingsAmount at services/workspaces.py:153). required_clients() (line 30) returns ('workspaces',) only; there is no CloudWatch client or metric read in either file. The module comment lines 15-17 self-admits savings 'depend on user-login patterns the adapter doesn't measure.' The flat config-derived fabricated-$ mechanism is demonstrated in real code. Caveat: the specific live-pricing economics cited (Power AutoStop $19/mo + $0.68/hr, break-even ~87 hrs, heavy user pays ~$48 more) are illustrative and not independently verified here, but they do not affect the confirmed code-level mechanism.

#### 🟠 C3 · billing_mode & unused recs carry no ComputeType, so counted savings always defaults to STANDARD ($10.50) regardless of real bundle  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/adapters/workspaces.py:53-66`
- **Evidence:** scan() resolves compute_type = rec.get("ComputeType",""); if falsy -> rec.get("WorkspaceProperties",{}).get("ComputeTypeName","STANDARD"). But the billing_mode_optimization dict (services/workspaces.py:98-107) and unused_workspaces dict (services/workspaces.py:111-119) contain NEITHER a ComputeType key NOR a WorkspaceProperties key. So compute_type always resolves to "STANDARD" and the counted saving is always WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY["STANDARD"]=35 * mult * 0.30 = $10.50.
- **Impact:** A GRAPHICSPRO ($999 live) or POWERPRO ($140 live) ALWAYS_ON / stopped WorkSpace is counted at the STANDARD AutoStop saving ($10.50), grossly understating large bundles and overstating VALUE ($25). The brief's stated formula (bundle[ComputeType]*mult*0.30) never actually varies by bundle for these two checks.
- **Fix:** Propagate the real ComputeTypeName from the discovered WorkspaceProperties into the billing_mode_optimization and unused_workspaces rec dicts in services/workspaces.py so scan() prices the actual bundle (or move the whole computation into the shim).
- **Verifier (confirmed):** services/adapters/workspaces.py:54-57 resolves compute_type = rec.get('ComputeType','') and, if falsy, rec.get('WorkspaceProperties',{}).get('ComputeTypeName','STANDARD'). The billing_mode_optimization dict (services/workspaces.py:98-107) and unused_workspaces dict (services/workspaces.py:112-119) contain NEITHER a ComputeType key NOR a WorkspaceProperties key — verified by reading both dict literals. The real bundle is read at services/workspaces.py:124 for the rightsizing path but is never propagated into these two rec dicts. Therefore compute_type always resolves to 'STANDARD', and since these recs never carry EstimatedSavingsAmount they hit the else branch: WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY['STANDARD']=35 (services/workspaces.py:31) * mult * 0.30 = $10.50 regardless of true bundle. A GRAPHICSPRO ($735, line 36) or POWERPRO ($124, line 34) is undercounted; VALUE ($25, line 30) is overcounted. Confirmed exactly as described.

#### 🟠 C5 · STOPPED/AUTO_STOP WorkSpaces flagged as 'Full workspace monthly cost' though they already bill only the small monthly fee  ·  `confirmed_bug` — **✅ confirmed**
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:110-120`
- **Evidence:** unused_workspaces triggers on State in {STOPPED,ERROR,SUSPENDED} with no check of RunningMode (running_mode is captured at line 94 and stored at line 115 but never gates the saving). A STOPPED WorkSpace with RunningMode==AUTO_STOP bills only the fixed monthly fee (live: Power AutoStop fee = $19/mo; SKU YE55FXMUCR7VAU2K) and $0 hourly while stopped, yet it is counted at STANDARD*mult*0.30 = $10.50 of fabricated saving.
- **Impact:** False-positive savings on an already-cheap (scaled-to-zero-equivalent) resource — the WorkSpaces analogue of the EKS 0-node / scaled-to-zero trap. Only ALWAYS_ON-stopped WorkSpaces still bill near full and warrant a termination saving.
- **Fix:** Distinguish RunningMode: for STOPPED+AUTO_STOP either drop the rec or count only the residual monthly fee + storage; reserve the near-full-cost termination saving for ALWAYS_ON-stopped WorkSpaces.
- **Verifier (confirmed):** services/workspaces.py:110 gates unused_workspaces solely on state in ['STOPPED','ERROR','SUSPENDED']; running_mode is captured at line 94 and merely stored in the rec at line 115 ('RunningMode': running_mode) but never used in any conditional that affects the saving. The adapter then counts it (via C3's STANDARD default) at 35*mult*0.30=$10.50. So a STOPPED workspace whose RunningMode is AUTO_STOP — which bills only the fixed monthly fee and $0 hourly while stopped — is credited a termination saving identical to a near-full-cost ALWAYS_ON workspace; the EstimatedSavings display text 'Full workspace monthly cost' (line 117) further overstates it. Code mechanism (no RunningMode gate) confirmed; the AUTO_STOP-billing economics are correct AWS behavior though the exact fee figure ($19) is not independently verified here and does not change the confirmed mechanism. Distinct from C3 (defaulted bundle) — this is the separate scaled-to-zero false-positive.

#### 🟡 C4 · Display-vs-counted desync: cards show fabricated "$50/month" and "Full workspace monthly cost" while headline counts $10.50  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:104,117`
- **Evidence:** billing_mode rec sets EstimatedSavings="$50/month potential per workspace" (line 104) — $50 appears in NO price table (WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY has no 50 entry; confirmed not derivable). unused rec sets EstimatedSavings="Full workspace monthly cost" (line 117). The generic Phase B renderer prints rec["EstimatedSavings"] verbatim (reporter_phase_b.py:1803-1804) while the headline counts scan()'s $10.50 (see C3). _calculate_service_savings returns the canonical total (html_report_generator.py:3078-3079), so card text and headline diverge.
- **Impact:** Counted==rendered holds for COUNT (every rec renders via the WorkspaceId per-rec fallback) but the per-card dollar figure contradicts the executive-summary contribution — $50 shown, $10.50 counted, and 'Full workspace monthly cost' shown while only 30% counted.
- **Fix:** Set EstimatedSavings/EstimatedSavingsAmount to the same concrete number scan() counts (after C3 fix), removing the fabricated $50 and the 'Full cost' string; render the delta the headline uses.

#### 🟡 C6 · Intra-adapter double count: one AVAILABLE+ALWAYS_ON over-ranked WorkSpace counted in both billing_mode_optimization and bundle_rightsizing  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:96,122-156`
- **Evidence:** The State=="AVAILABLE"&&ALWAYS_ON gate (line 96) and the State=="AVAILABLE"&&rank>=3 gate (line 122) are not mutually exclusive; a POWER ALWAYS_ON WorkSpace matches both and both recs are appended to all_recommendations. scan() counts billing_mode via the 0.30 fallback ($10.50, see C3) AND bundle_rightsizing via EstimatedSavingsAmount (e.g. POWER 80 - PERFORMANCE 60 = $20), summing $30.50 of savings against one WorkSpace whose actual AlwaysOn bill is ~$80.
- **Impact:** Switching to AutoStop and downsizing the bundle discount the SAME monthly bill; counting them additively at face value overstates the per-WorkSpace opportunity (catalogue: two heuristic levers stacking on one resource).
- **Fix:** Pick one lever per WorkSpace (rightsize first, then AutoStop on the smaller bundle) or compute a combined, non-additive saving; add the WorkSpace to a covered set after the first counted rec.

#### 🟡 C7 · Stale WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY constants: PowerPro and GraphicsPro understated ~11% / ~26% vs live AWS prices  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:29-37`
- **Evidence:** Table: POWERPRO=124.0, GRAPHICSPRO=735.0. Live AWS Pricing API us-east-1 AlwaysOn/Windows/Included: PowerPro full bundle = $140.00/Month (SKU 9M7TNDXEHK432522, '8vCPU,32GB,175GB Root,100GB User'); GraphicsPro full bundle = $999.00/Month (SKU 4GQGYJZHP5W278AE, '16vCPU,122GB,8GB GPU'). 124 vs 140 = -11.4%; 735 vs 999 = -26.4%. (GraphicsPro.g4dn variant = $959, SKU SAXMZ7UAX736ARQ5.)
- **Impact:** bundle_rightsizing deltas built from these constants understate savings for GRAPHICS/GRAPHICSPRO/POWERPRO downgrades. VALUE/STANDARD/PERFORMANCE (25/35/60) were not live-validated this run; STANDARD is the de-facto rate for ALL billing_mode/unused counts (see C3) so its accuracy is load-bearing and should also be re-checked.
- **Fix:** Refresh the constants from the live AlwaysOn/Windows/Included full-bundle rows (PowerPro 140, GraphicsPro 999, GraphicsPro.g4dn 959) and add a dated provenance/AuditBasis comment; schedule periodic re-validation since the API first-row lookup is non-deterministic.

#### 🟡 M1 · bundle_rightsizing target depends on ctx.pricing_engine truthiness (unrelated to pricing) and contains dead branch code  ·  `confirmed_bug`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:130-133`
- **Evidence:** Line 130-131: `if current_rank >= 4 and ctx.pricing_engine: target_type = "STANDARD"`. Pricing here uses the static WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY table (_get_bundle_price_by_compute_type), NOT the engine, so gating the recommended target on engine truthiness is arbitrary: a GRAPHICSPRO is offered STANDARD when an engine is present but only PERFORMANCE when it is absent. Line 133: `target_type = "PERFORMANCE" if current_rank > 2 else None` is reached only when current_rank>=3, so `> 2` is always True and the `else None` is dead code.
- **Impact:** Same input WorkSpace yields a different downgrade target (and thus a different counted saving, e.g. GRAPHICSPRO->STANDARD saves $700 vs ->PERFORMANCE $675) based on an unrelated flag; reveals confused intent and a non-deterministic recommendation.
- **Fix:** Choose the rightsizing target purely from rank/utilization evidence (decouple from ctx.pricing_engine) and delete the unreachable `else None`.

#### 🟡 M2 · bundle_rightsizing asserts a 'utilization profile' while reading no utilization metric  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:149-151`
- **Evidence:** Recommendation text: f"Downgrade from {compute_type} to {target_type} based on utilization profile" (line 150). The adapter reads only describe_workspaces config — no CloudWatch, no CPU/session metric anywhere (required_clients=("workspaces",)).
- **Impact:** Recommends a downsize as if usage-justified with zero usage evidence (catalogue: 'heuristic that assumes a usage target with no evidence'); a fully-utilized POWER WorkSpace would be wrongly told to downgrade.
- **Fix:** Either gate on AWS/WorkSpaces CPU/session metrics, or reword to an explicit config-only advisory and demote to $0/Counted=False until evidence exists.

#### 🟢 L1 · Bundle table is Windows + License-Included only; OS/license/storage variants mispriced  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/workspaces.py:23-37,63-73`
- **Evidence:** Header comment (lines 23-24) states the table is 'us-east-1, Windows w/ Plus bundle'. compute_type-only lookup ignores operatingSystem and license. Live API confirms divergent SKUs: BYOL (license 'Bring Your Own License'), Linux/Ubuntu, and storage variants (Root/User GB) all bill differently; the AmazonWorkSpaces license dimension includes 'Bring Your Own License' and 'Included'.
- **Impact:** Accounts with BYOL or Linux/Ubuntu WorkSpaces (or non-default storage) get Windows+Included prices, skewing every counted saving. Lower severity because most fleets are Windows+Included.
- **Fix:** Key the price lookup on (compute_type, operatingSystem, license) read from each WorkSpace, or scope the recommendation to Windows+Included and skip others.

#### 🟢 L2 · services/adapters/CLAUDE.md lists a dead pricing method for workspaces.py  ·  `limitation`
- **Location:** `services/adapters/CLAUDE.md:Live-Pricing table, workspaces.py row`
- **Evidence:** Row reads: `workspaces.py | get_instance_monthly_price("AmazonWorkSpaces", ...) | AWS Pricing API`. Live API confirms AmazonWorkSpaces has NO instanceType attribute (filterable dims: bundle, runningMode, license, operatingSystem, pricingUnit, memory, vcpu, storage, ...), so that method structurally returns 0. The adapter actually uses the hardcoded WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY table (services/adapters/workspaces.py:45-66; docstring lines 47-51).
- **Impact:** Documentation misrepresents the pricing source; an engineer trusting the row would look for a live lookup that does not exist. Doc-only, no runtime cost impact.
- **Fix:** Update the row to: 'WORKSPACE_BUNDLE_MONTHLY hardcoded us-east-1 Windows+Included table, region-scaled by pricing_multiplier (AmazonWorkSpaces Pricing API has no instanceType attribute; bundle rows commingle $0 base + software add-ons).'
